BRA_increase_adhemar_corruption_idea = {
	if = {
		limit = { has_idea = BRA_squeaky_clean_idea }
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = BRA_squeaky_clean_idea
			add_idea = BRA_a_handshake_here_and_there_idea
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_idea = BRA_a_handshake_here_and_there_idea }
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = BRA_a_handshake_here_and_there_idea
			add_idea = BRA_the_reality_of_governance_idea
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_idea = BRA_the_reality_of_governance_idea }
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = BRA_the_reality_of_governance_idea
			add_idea = BRA_dirty_hands_idea
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_idea = BRA_dirty_hands_idea }
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = BRA_dirty_hands_idea
			add_idea = BRA_ruled_by_favours_idea
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_idea = BRA_ruled_by_favours_idea }
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = BRA_ruled_by_favours_idea
			add_idea = BRA_conmans_paradise_idea
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_idea = BRA_conmans_paradise_idea }
		custom_effect_tooltip = BRA_adhemar_max_corruption_idea_tt
	}
}
BRA_decrease_adhemar_corruption_idea = {
	if = {
		limit = { has_idea = BRA_conmans_paradise_idea }
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = BRA_conmans_paradise_idea
			add_idea = BRA_ruled_by_favours_idea
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_idea = BRA_ruled_by_favours_idea }
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = BRA_ruled_by_favours_idea
			add_idea = BRA_dirty_hands_idea
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_idea = BRA_dirty_hands_idea }
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = BRA_dirty_hands_idea
			add_idea = BRA_the_reality_of_governance_idea
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_idea = BRA_the_reality_of_governance_idea }
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = BRA_the_reality_of_governance_idea
			add_idea = BRA_a_handshake_here_and_there_idea
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_idea = BRA_a_handshake_here_and_there_idea }
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = BRA_a_handshake_here_and_there_idea
			add_idea = BRA_squeaky_clean_idea
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_idea = BRA_squeaky_clean_idea }
		custom_effect_tooltip = BRA_adhemar_min_corruption_idea_tt
	}
}
BRA_count_denys_coup_triggers = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				check_variable = { BRA_military_const_power < BRA_military_sorbonne_power }
				check_variable = { BRA_military_const_power < BRA_military_hardliners_power }
			}
		}
		add_to_variable = { BRA_denys_coup_trigger = 1 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { BRA_military_sorbonne_power < BRA_military_hardliners_power }
			}
			add_to_variable = { BRA_denys_coup_trigger = 1 }
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { BRA_military_loyalty < 20 }
		}
		add_to_variable = { BRA_denys_coup_trigger = 1 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { BRA_military_nepotism > 69 }
		}
		add_to_variable = { BRA_denys_coup_trigger = 1 }
	}
}

BRA_create_leader_denys = {
	BRA_Odilio_Denys = {
		promote_character = yes
	}
	remove_all_ministers = yes
	add_ideas = {
		BRA_Auro_de_Moura_Andrade_hog
		BRA_Juracy_Magalhaes_for
		BRA_Delfim_Netto_eco
		BRA_Amaury_Kruel_sec
	}
	add_popularity = {
		ideology = despotism
		popularity = 0.2
	}
}

BRA_create_leader_quadros = {
	if = {
		limit = { BRA_Janio_Quadros = { NOT = { has_ideology = conservatism_populist_conservatism_subtype } } }
		add_country_leader_role = {
			character = BRA_Janio_Quadros
			promote_leader = yes
			country_leader = {
				desc = "POLITICS_JANIO_QUADROS_DESC"
				expire = "1994.4.20"
				ideology = conservatism_populist_conservatism_subtype
				traits = { man_of_the_broom_latin }
				id = -1
			}
		}
	}
	set_party_name = {
		ideology = conservatism
		long_name = BRA_conservatism_party_long
		name = BRA_conservatism_party
	}
}

BRA_create_leader_adhemar = {
	hidden_effect = {
		set_variable = {
			BRA_Corruption = 0.5
		}
		set_party_name = {
			ideology = paternalism
			long_name = BRA_paternalism_party_long
			name = BRA_paternalism_party
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { BRA_Adhemar_de_Barros = { NOT = { has_ideology = paternalism_right_wing_populism_subtype } } }
		add_country_leader_role = {
			character = BRA_Adhemar_de_Barros
			promote_leader = yes
			country_leader = {
				desc = "POLITICS_ADHEMAR_DE_BARROS_DESC"
				expire = "1994.4.20"
				ideology = paternalism_right_wing_populism_subtype
				traits = { playful_populist_latin }
				id = -1
			}
		}
	}
	BRA_corruption_refresh = yes
	add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = BRA_corruption_level }
}

BRA_reload_tree = {
	custom_effect_tooltip = TNO_focus_tree_reload_tt
	mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes
}

BRA_hundred_days_crisis_begins = { # a
	if = {
		limit = { has_idea = BRA_Janio_Quadros_hog }
		remove_ideas = BRA_Janio_Quadros_hog
	}
	clr_country_flag = BRA_quadros_wins_hundred_days

	set_party_name = {
		ideology = despotism
		long_name = BRA_despotism_party_gridlock_long
		name = BRA_despotism_party_gridlock
	}
	set_politics = {
		ruling_party = despotism
		elections_allowed = yes #not yet
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = { has_country_leader = { character = BRA_Auro_de_Moura_Andrade } }
		}

		add_country_leader_role = {
			character = BRA_Auro_de_Moura_Andrade
			promote_leader = yes
			country_leader = {
				desc = "POLITICS_AURO_DE_MOURA_ANDRADE_DESC"
				expire = "1994.4.20"
				ideology = despotism_interim_government_subtype
				traits = { cattle_king_latin }
				id = -1
			}
		}
	}
	swap_ideas = {
		remove_idea = BRA_the_populist_republic
		add_idea = BRA_hundred_days
	}
	custom_effect_tooltip = BRA_new_cabinet_tt
	hidden_effect = {
		remove_all_ministers = yes
		add_ideas = {
			BRA_Pascoal_Ranieri_Mazzilli_hog
			BRA_Vasco_Leitao_da_Cunha_adhemar_for
			BRA_Generic_Vacant_eco
			BRA_Generic_Vacant_sec
		}
	}
	set_country_flag = BRA_hundred_days_crisis_begun
	load_focus_tree = { tree = BRA_Hundred_Days_Crisis_tree }
	mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes

	clr_country_flag = BRA_lottquadros_category_allowed

	set_country_flag = BRA_hundred_days_category_allowed
	BRA_initialize_hundred_days_mechanic = yes

	hidden_effect = {
		country_event = { id = brazil.337 days = 14 }
		every_country = {
			limit = { is_ai = no }
			news_event = {
				id = LATAM_news.11
			}
		}
	}
}

BRA_quadros_wins_hundred_days = {
	remove_ideas = BRA_Janio_Quadros_hog
	hidden_effect = {
			add_ideas = BRA_Generic_Vacant_hog
		}
	set_politics = {
		ruling_party = conservatism
		elections_allowed = yes
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = { has_country_leader = { character = BRA_Janio_Quadros } }
		}
		BRA_create_leader_quadros = yes
		add_timed_idea = {
			idea = BRA_democracy_survives
			days = 50
		}
	}

	load_focus_tree = { tree = BRA_Quadros_Coup_tree }

	clr_country_flag = BRA_lottquadros_category_allowed

	set_country_flag = BRA_quadros_wins_hundred_days

	clr_country_flag = BRA_hundred_days_category_allowed
}

d_BRA_lacerda_udn_management_initiate = {
	BRA = { BRA_lacerda_udn_management_initiate = yes }
}
BRA_lacerda_udn_management_initiate = {
	set_country_flag = BRA_UDN_management_GUI_visible
	set_variable = { BRA_lacerda_udn_manage_econ = 22.5 }
	set_variable = { BRA_lacerda_udn_manage_pol = -20 }
	set_variable = { BRA_lacerda_samba_project_boost = 0.05 }

	set_variable = { BRA_lacerda_udn_manage_econ_min = -100 }
	set_variable = { BRA_lacerda_udn_manage_pol_min = -100 }

	set_variable = { BRA_lacerda_udn_manage_econ_max = 100 }
	set_variable = { BRA_lacerda_udn_manage_pol_max = 100 }

	set_variable = { BRA_lacerda_udn_manage_econ_tick = 0 }
	set_variable = { BRA_lacerda_udn_manage_pol_tick = 0 }

	set_variable = { BRA_lacerda_udn_manage_unity = 80 }
	set_variable = { BRA_lacerda_udn_manage_unity_max = 100 }

	set_variable = { BRA_udn_pp_gain = 0.05 }

	set_variable = { BRA_monthly_udn_loyalty = -4 }
	add_dynamic_modifier = {
		modifier = BRA_udn_manage_dynmod
	}
	BRA_lacerda_udn_management_calculate_dot_pos = yes
	activate_mission = BRA_lacerda_unity_change_mission
}

BRA_lacerda_udn_unity_change = { # USE THIS WHEN MODYFING UDN LOYALTY!!! ZAMN!!!
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { temp_udn_unity < 0 }
		}
		multiply_temp_variable = { temp_udn_unity = -1 }
		BRA_lacerda_udn_unity_decrease = yes
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { temp_udn_unity > 0 }
		}
		BRA_lacerda_udn_unity_increase = yes
	}
	clamp_variable = {
		var = BRA_lacerda_udn_manage_unity
		min = 0
		max = BRA_lacerda_udn_manage_unity_max
	}
	hidden_effect = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				BRA_lacerda_udn_manage_unity < 60
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = BRA_lacerda_udn_unloyal
				}
			}
			country_event = {
				id = brazil_lacerda_udn.1
				days = 30
			}
		}
		else = {
			BRA_lacerda_party_switch_trigger = yes
		}
	}
	}
}

BRA_lacerda_party_switch_trigger = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				BRA_lacerda_udn_manage_unity < 20
			}
		}
		activate_mission = BRA_lacerda_party_switch_mission_90
	}
}

BRA_lacerda_udn_unity_increase = {
	add_to_variable = { BRA_lacerda_udn_manage_unity = temp_udn_unity }
	custom_effect_tooltip = BRA_lacerda_udn_unity_increase_tt
}

BRA_lacerda_udn_unity_decrease = {
	subtract_from_variable = { BRA_lacerda_udn_manage_unity = temp_udn_unity }
	custom_effect_tooltip = BRA_lacerda_udn_unity_decrease_tt
}

	custom_effect_tooltip = BRA_lott_deal_if_signed
	effect_tooltip = {

			add_political_power = 40
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = BRA_idea_RK_settlement
				add_idea = BRA_idea_RK_settlement_good_cg
			}
		}
		COG = {
			add_political_power = -40
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = BRA_idea_RK_settlement
				add_idea = BRA_idea_RK_settlement_bad_cg
			}
		}
	}
	custom_effect_tooltip = BRA_lott_deal_if_signed_spacing
	BRA = { set_variable = { BRA_lott_deal_fish = 0 } }
}

		}
	}
	custom_effect_tooltip = BRA_lott_deal_if_signed_spacing
	BRA = { set_variable = { BRA_lott_deal_return = 0 } }
}

###############################################################
########        Adhemar Personal Wealth Mechanic       ########
###############################################################

# Initialization
BRA_adhemar_moneybags_initialization = {
	if = {
		limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = BRA_adhemar_moneybags_category_allowed } }
		custom_effect_tooltip = BRA_adhemar_moneybags_initialization_tt
		set_variable = { BRA_adhemar_wealth = 5 }
		set_variable = { BRA_adhemar_legacy = 0 }

		BRA_redraw_moneybags_wealth = yes

		set_country_flag = BRA_adhemar_moneybags_category_allowed
	}
}

BRA_redraw_moneybags_wealth = {

	clear_array = BRA_adhemar_wealth_numbers
	clear_array = BRA_adhemar_wealth_offsets

	set_temp_variable = { wealth = BRA_adhemar_wealth }
	multiply_temp_variable = { wealth = 10 }
	subtract_from_temp_variable = { wealth = 0.5 }
	round_temp_variable = wealth
	set_temp_variable = { offset = 0 }

	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { BRA_adhemar_wealth < 10 }
		}
		set_temp_variable = { current_digit = wealth }
		modulo_temp_variable = { current_digit = 10 }
		add_to_temp_variable = { current_digit = 1 }
		add_to_array = {
			array = BRA_adhemar_wealth_numbers
			value = current_digit
			index = 0
		}
		add_to_array = {
			array = BRA_adhemar_wealth_numbers
			value = 11
			index = 0
		}
		add_to_array = { BRA_adhemar_wealth_offsets = 0 }
		add_to_array = { BRA_adhemar_wealth_offsets = 0 }

		set_temp_variable = { offset = 8 }
	}

	set_temp_variable = { wealth = BRA_adhemar_wealth }
	subtract_from_temp_variable = { wealth = 0.5 }
	round_temp_variable = wealth

	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { wealth < 1 } }
		add_to_array = {
			array = BRA_adhemar_wealth_numbers
			value = 0
			index = 0
		}
		add_to_array = {
			array = BRA_adhemar_wealth_offsets
			value = offset
			index = 0
		}
	}
	while_loop_effect = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { wealth > 0 }
		}


		set_temp_variable = { current_digit = wealth }
		modulo_temp_variable = { current_digit = 10 }
		subtract_from_temp_variable = { wealth = current_digit }
		divide_temp_variable = { wealth = 10 }

		add_to_temp_variable = { current_digit = 1 }
		add_to_array = {
			array = BRA_adhemar_wealth_numbers
			value = current_digit
			index = 0
		}
		add_to_array = {
			array = BRA_adhemar_wealth_offsets
			value = offset
			index = 0
		}
	}

	set_variable = { BRA_adhemar_wealth_frame = 1 }
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { BRA_adhemar_wealth > 24.99 } }
		set_variable = { BRA_adhemar_wealth_frame = 2 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { BRA_adhemar_wealth > 49.99 } }
		set_variable = { BRA_adhemar_wealth_frame = 3 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { BRA_adhemar_wealth > 99.99 } }
		set_variable = { BRA_adhemar_wealth_frame = 4 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { BRA_adhemar_wealth > 149.99 } }
		set_variable = { BRA_adhemar_wealth_frame = 5 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { BRA_adhemar_wealth > 199.99 } }
		set_variable = { BRA_adhemar_wealth_frame = 6 }
	}

	set_variable = { BRA_adhemar_portrait_frame = 1 }
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { BRA_adhemar_wealth > 24.99} }
		set_variable = { BRA_adhemar_portrait_frame = 2 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { BRA_adhemar_wealth > 99.99 } }
		set_variable = { BRA_adhemar_portrait_frame = 3 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { BRA_adhemar_wealth > 149.99 } }
		set_variable = { BRA_adhemar_portrait_frame = 4 }
	}


	set_variable = { BRA_adhemar_legacy_frame = BRA_adhemar_legacy }
	add_to_variable = { BRA_adhemar_legacy_frame = 3 }
	clamp_variable = { var = BRA_adhemar_legacy_frame min = 1 max = 7 }
	subtract_from_variable = { BRA_adhemar_legacy_frame = 0.5 }
	round_variable = BRA_adhemar_legacy_frame




	set_temp_variable = { wealth_offset_position = BRA_adhemar_wealth_numbers^num }

	multiply_temp_variable = { wealth_offset_position = -7.5 }
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { offset > 0 } }
		subtract_from_temp_variable = { wealth_offset_position = 4 }
	}

	log = "[?wealth_offset_position]"
	for_each_loop = {
		array = BRA_adhemar_wealth_numbers
		index = idx

		add_to_variable = { BRA_adhemar_wealth_offsets^idx = wealth_offset_position }
		log = "[?BRA_adhemar_wealth_offsets^idx]"
	}


	set_variable = { BRA_adhemar_wealth_m_position = BRA_adhemar_wealth_numbers^num }
	multiply_variable = { BRA_adhemar_wealth_m_position = 15 }
	add_to_variable = { BRA_adhemar_wealth_m_position = wealth_offset_position }
}

BRA_set_central_bank_policy_slush_fund = {
	custom_effect_tooltip = BRA_set_central_bank_policy_slush_fund_tt
	hidden_effect = {
		set_variable = { BRA_previous_central_bank_policy = selected_central_bank_id }
		add_to_array = { central_bank_policies_array = 4 }
		set_temp_variable = { temp_selected_central_bank_id = 4 }
		set_variable = { selected_central_bank_id = temp_selected_central_bank_id }
		add_to_variable = { TNO_economy_GUI_dirty = 1 }
		clr_country_flag = central_bank_policies_tab_open
		set_variable = { econ_tab_central_bank_display_policy_btn_frame = 1 }
	}
}


BRA_clear_central_bank_policy_slush_fund = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			is_in_array = { central_bank_policies_array = 4 }
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = BRA_clear_central_bank_policy_slush_fund_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { BRA_previous_central_bank_policy = 4 }
				}
				set_variable = { BRA_previous_central_bank_policy = 1 }
			}
			set_temp_variable = { temp_selected_central_bank_id = BRA_previous_central_bank_policy }
			set_variable = { selected_central_bank_id = BRA_previous_central_bank_policy }

			remove_from_array = { central_bank_policies_array = 4 }
			add_to_variable = { TNO_economy_GUI_dirty = 1 }

			clr_country_flag = central_bank_policies_tab_open
			set_variable = { econ_tab_central_bank_display_policy_btn_frame = 1 }
		}
	}
}

######## 			Other Adhemar Effects 			   ########

BRA_Muller_switches_PSP = {
	set_country_flag = BRA_adhemar_muller_switched
	custom_effect_tooltip = BRA_Muller_switches_PSP_tooltip
	hidden_effect = {
		set_temp_variable = { tmp_to_party = 4 }
		set_temp_variable = { tmp_senator = 28 }
		BRA_switch_parties_one = yes
		set_variable = { BRA_identities_parties^28 = 4 } #failsafe to ensure he switches party in elections
	}
}

BRA_adhemar_coma_random_events = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				BRA_adhemar_coma_random_events_num > BRA_adhemar_coma_turns
			}
		}
		country_event = { id = brazil_adhemar_coma.2901 }
	}
	else = {
		random_list = {
			1 = {
				modifier = {
					factor = 0
					OR = {
						has_country_flag = brazil_adhemar_coma.2301_triggered
						NOT = { has_country_flag = BRA_Healthcare_Bill_Passed }
					}
				}
				country_event = { id = brazil_adhemar_coma.2301 days = 3 }
			}
			1 = {
				modifier = {
					factor = 0
					OR = {
						has_country_flag = brazil_adhemar_coma.23_triggered
						NOT = { has_country_flag = BRA_Adhemar_education_bill_Passed }
					}
				}
				country_event = { id = brazil_adhemar_coma.23 days = 3 }
			}
			1 = {
				modifier = {
					factor = 0
					OR = {
						has_country_flag = brazil_adhemar_coma.24_triggered
						NOT = { has_country_flag = BRA_Adhemar_social_security_bill_Passed }
					}
				}
				country_event = { id = brazil_adhemar_coma.24 days = 3 }
			}
			1 = {
				modifier = {
					factor = 0
					NOT = { has_country_flag = brazil_adhemar_coma.25_triggered } #Triggers for not meeting industrialisation results
				}
				country_event = { id = brazil_adhemar_coma.25 days = 3 }
			}
			1 = {
				modifier = {
					factor = 0
					OR = {
						has_country_flag = brazil_adhemar_coma.26_triggered
						NOT = {
							AND = {
								has_country_flag = BRA_pspobras_completed
								has_country_flag = BRA_and_his_ideas_completed
							}
						}
					}
				}
				country_event = { id = brazil_adhemar_coma.26 days = 3 }
			}
			1 = {
				modifier = {
					factor = 0
					OR = {
						has_country_flag = brazil_adhemar_coma.27_triggered
						NOT = { has_country_flag = BRA_adhemar_won_the_100_days }
					}
				}
				country_event = { id = brazil_adhemar_coma.27 days = 3 }
			}
			1 = {
				modifier = {
					factor = 0
					OR = {
						has_country_flag = brazil_adhemar_coma.29_triggered
						NOT = { has_country_flag = BRA_SACW_Nukes_developed }
					}
				}
				country_event = { id = brazil_adhemar_coma.29 days = 3 }
			}
			1 = {
				modifier = {
					factor = 0
					OR = {
						has_country_flag = brazil_adhemar_coma.28_triggered
						NOT = { has_completed_focus = BRA_exercito_social_progressista }
					}
				}
				country_event = { id = brazil_adhemar_coma.28 days = 3 }
			}
		}
	}
}



###############################################################
########             Hundred Days Mechanic             ########
###############################################################

BRA_initialize_hundred_days_mechanic = {
	set_variable = { BRA_hd_adhemar_support = BRA_PSP_seats }
	set_variable = { BRA_hd_lacerda_support = BRA_UDN_seats }
	set_variable = { BRA_hd_goulart_support = BRA_PTB_seats }
	set_variable = { BRA_hd_kubitschek_support = BRA_PSD_seats }
	add_to_variable = { BRA_hd_adhemar_support = 10 }

	BRA_update_hundred_days = yes
}

BRA_hundred_days_randomize_competitor = {
	set_variable = { BRA_hd_competitor = random }
	multiply_variable = { BRA_hd_competitor = 3 }
	subtract_from_variable = { BRA_hd_competitor = 0.5 }
	round_variable = BRA_hd_competitor

	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = BRA_hd_chose_adhemar
		}
		add_to_variable = { BRA_hd_competitor = 1 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = BRA_hd_chose_lacerda
			check_variable = { BRA_hd_competitor > 0 }
		}
		add_to_variable = { BRA_hd_competitor = 1 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = BRA_hd_conference_chose_goulart
			check_variable = { BRA_hd_competitor > 1 }
		}
		add_to_variable = { BRA_hd_competitor = 1 }
	}

	log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Competitor set to [?BRA_hd_competitor]"
}

BRA_update_hundred_days = {
	clamp_variable = { var = BRA_hd_adhemar_support min = 0 max = 100 }
	clamp_variable = { var = BRA_hd_lacerda_support min = 0 max = 100 }
	clamp_variable = { var = BRA_hd_goulart_support min = 0 max = 100 }
	clamp_variable = { var = BRA_hd_kubitschek_support min = 0 max = 100 }

	set_temp_variable = { total = BRA_hd_adhemar_support }
	add_to_temp_variable = { total = BRA_hd_lacerda_support }
	add_to_temp_variable = { total = BRA_hd_goulart_support }
	add_to_temp_variable = { total = BRA_hd_kubitschek_support }

	divide_temp_variable = { total = 100 }
	divide_variable = { BRA_hd_adhemar_support = total }
	divide_variable = { BRA_hd_lacerda_support = total }
	divide_variable = { BRA_hd_goulart_support = total }
	divide_variable = { BRA_hd_kubitschek_support = total }

	set_variable = { BRA_hd_pie3_progress = BRA_hd_goulart_support }
	set_variable = { BRA_hd_pie2_progress = BRA_hd_pie3_progress }
	add_to_variable = { BRA_hd_pie2_progress = BRA_hd_adhemar_support }
	set_variable = { BRA_hd_pie1_progress = BRA_hd_pie2_progress }
	add_to_variable = { BRA_hd_pie1_progress = BRA_hd_lacerda_support }
}

	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { BRA_pl_current_bill_id = 0 } }
		custom_effect_tooltip = BRA_pl_increase_ptb_support_pct_low_natfoc
	}
	else = {
		custom_effect_tooltip = BRA_pl_increase_ptb_support_pct_low
	}
	add_to_variable = { BRA_pl_ptb_support_pct = 0.05 }
	BRA_update_pl = yes
}

BRA_initialize_bill = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { BRA_pl_current_bill_id = 0 }
		}
		set_variable = { BRA_pl_current_bill_id = temp_bill }
		set_country_flag = BRA_pl_visible

		set_variable = { BRA_pl_ptb_supporters_modifier = 0 }
		set_variable = { BRA_pl_psd_supporters_modifier = 0 }
		set_variable = { BRA_pl_udn_supporters_modifier = 0 }
		set_variable = { BRA_pl_psp_supporters_modifier = 0 }
		set_variable = { BRA_pl_prp_supporters_modifier = 0 }

		set_variable = { BRA_pl_ptb_support_pct = BRA_pl_ptb_support_bill@var:temp_bill }
		set_variable = { BRA_pl_psd_support_pct = BRA_pl_psd_support_bill@var:temp_bill }
		set_variable = { BRA_pl_udn_support_pct = BRA_pl_udn_support_bill@var:temp_bill }
		set_variable = { BRA_pl_psp_support_pct = BRA_pl_psp_support_bill@var:temp_bill }
		set_variable = { BRA_pl_prp_support_pct = BRA_pl_prp_support_bill@var:temp_bill }

		multiply_variable = { BRA_pl_ptb_support_pct = BRA_pl_ptb_modifier_lacerda } # for lacerda but can be easily universalised
		multiply_variable = { BRA_pl_psd_support_pct = BRA_pl_psd_modifier_lacerda }

		clamp_variable = { var = BRA_pl_ptb_support_pct min = BRA_pl_ptb_support_pct_min max = BRA_pl_ptb_support_pct_max }
		clamp_variable = { var = BRA_pl_psd_support_pct min = BRA_pl_psd_support_pct_min max = BRA_pl_psd_support_pct_max }
		clamp_variable = { var = BRA_pl_udn_support_pct min = BRA_pl_udn_support_pct_min max = BRA_pl_udn_support_pct_max }
		clamp_variable = { var = BRA_pl_psp_support_pct min = BRA_pl_psp_support_pct_min max = BRA_pl_psp_support_pct_max }
		clamp_variable = { var = BRA_pl_prp_support_pct min = BRA_pl_prp_support_pct_min max = BRA_pl_prp_support_pct_max }

		set_variable = { BRA_pl_bill_id = temp_bill }
		BRA_update_pl = yes
		custom_effect_tooltip = BRA_pl_introduce_bill_tt
	}
	else = {
		add_to_array = { BRA_pl_bill_queue = temp_bill }
		custom_effect_tooltip = BRA_pl_add_bill_to_q_tt
	}
}

BRA_move_bill_from_queue = {
	set_temp_variable = { temp_bill = BRA_pl_bill_queue^0 }
	BRA_initialize_bill = yes
	set_variable = { BRA_pl_vote_days_var = BRA_pl_vote_days@var:BRA_pl_current_bill_id }
	set_country_flag = BRA_pl_voting
	set_country_flag = BRA_pl_voting_preview
	set_temp_variable = { alert_id = token:Alert_BRA_PLVoting }
	add_TNO_alert_unless_exists = yes
	custom_effect_tooltip = BRA_pl_call_bill_vote_tt
	remove_from_array = {
		array = BRA_pl_bill_queue
		index = 0
	}
}

BRA_call_bill_vote = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { BRA_pl_current_bill_id = temp_bill }
		}
		set_variable = { BRA_pl_vote_days_var = BRA_pl_vote_days@var:BRA_pl_current_bill_id }
		set_country_flag = BRA_pl_voting
		set_country_flag = BRA_pl_voting_preview

		set_temp_variable = { alert_id = token:Alert_BRA_PLVoting }
		add_TNO_alert_unless_exists = yes
		custom_effect_tooltip = BRA_pl_call_vote_tt
	}
}

BRA_interrupt_bill_vote = {
	clr_country_flag = BRA_pl_voting
	clr_country_flag = BRA_pl_voting_preview

	set_temp_variable = { alert_id = token:Alert_BRA_PLVoting }
	remove_TNO_alert = yes
}

BRA_give_up_on_bill = {
	clr_country_flag = BRA_pl_visible
	clr_country_flag = BRA_pl_voting
	clr_country_flag = BRA_pl_voting_preview
	set_variable = { BRA_pl_total_support = 0 }
	clear_variable = BRA_pl_current_bill_id

	set_temp_variable = { alert_id = token:Alert_BRA_PLVoting }
	remove_TNO_alert = yes
}

BRA_bill_complete = {
	set_temp_variable = { alert_id = token:Alert_BRA_PLVoting }
	remove_TNO_alert = yes

	BRA_update_pl = yes
	hidden_effect = {
		meta_effect = {
			text = { add_ideas = [IDEA] }
			IDEA = "[?BRA_pl_current_bill_id.GetTokenKey]"
		}
		# Clears any active decisions
		remove_decision = BRA_pl_rally_ptb
		remove_decision = BRA_pl_negotiate_ptb
		remove_decision = BRA_pl_rally_psd
		remove_decision = BRA_pl_negotiate_psd
		remove_decision = BRA_pl_rally_udn
		remove_decision = BRA_pl_negotiate_udn
		remove_decision = BRA_pl_rally_psp
		remove_decision = BRA_pl_negotiate_psp
		remove_decision = BRA_pl_rally_prp
		remove_decision = BRA_pl_negotiate_prp
		remove_decision = BRA_pl_bribe_ptb
		remove_decision = BRA_pl_bribe_psd
		remove_decision = BRA_pl_bribe_udn
		remove_decision = BRA_pl_bribe_psp
		remove_decision = BRA_pl_bribe_prp
	}
	clear_variable = BRA_pl_current_bill_id
	clear_variable = BRA_lacerda_pl_negotiations
}

BRA_update_pl = {

	set_temp_variable = { support_modifier = 1 }
	add_to_temp_variable = { support_modifier = modifier@BRA_bill_support }

	set_temp_variable = { modified_ptb_pct = BRA_pl_ptb_support_pct }
	multiply_temp_variable = { modified_ptb_pct = support_modifier }
	set_temp_variable = { modified_psd_pct = BRA_pl_psd_support_pct }
	multiply_temp_variable = { modified_psd_pct = support_modifier }
	set_temp_variable = { modified_udn_pct = BRA_pl_udn_support_pct }
	multiply_temp_variable = { modified_udn_pct = support_modifier }
	set_temp_variable = { modified_psp_pct = BRA_pl_psp_support_pct }
	multiply_temp_variable = { modified_psp_pct = support_modifier }
	set_temp_variable = { modified_prp_pct = BRA_pl_prp_support_pct }
	multiply_temp_variable = { modified_prp_pct = support_modifier }

	clamp_temp_variable = { var = modified_ptb_pct min = 0 max = 1 }
	clamp_temp_variable = { var = modified_psd_pct min = 0 max = 1 }
	clamp_temp_variable = { var = modified_udn_pct min = 0 max = 1 }
	clamp_temp_variable = { var = modified_psp_pct min = 0 max = 1 }
	clamp_temp_variable = { var = modified_prp_pct min = 0 max = 1 }

	set_variable = { BRA_pl_PTB_supporters_derived = BRA_PTB_seats }
	set_variable = { BRA_pl_PSD_supporters_derived = BRA_PSD_seats }
	set_variable = { BRA_pl_UDN_supporters_derived = BRA_UDN_seats }
	set_variable = { BRA_pl_PSP_supporters_derived = BRA_PSP_seats }
	set_variable = { BRA_pl_PRP_supporters_derived = BRA_PRP_seats }

	multiply_variable = { BRA_pl_PTB_supporters_derived = modified_ptb_pct }
	multiply_variable = { BRA_pl_PSD_supporters_derived = modified_psd_pct }
	multiply_variable = { BRA_pl_UDN_supporters_derived = modified_udn_pct }
	multiply_variable = { BRA_pl_PSP_supporters_derived = modified_psp_pct }
	multiply_variable = { BRA_pl_PRP_supporters_derived = modified_prp_pct }

	round_variable = BRA_pl_PTB_supporters_derived
	round_variable = BRA_pl_PSD_supporters_derived
	round_variable = BRA_pl_UDN_supporters_derived
	round_variable = BRA_pl_PSP_supporters_derived
	round_variable = BRA_pl_PRP_supporters_derived

	add_to_variable = { BRA_pl_PTB_supporters_derived = BRA_pl_ptb_supporters_modifier }
	add_to_variable = { BRA_pl_PSD_supporters_derived = BRA_pl_psd_supporters_modifier }
	add_to_variable = { BRA_pl_UDN_supporters_derived = BRA_pl_udn_supporters_modifier }
	add_to_variable = { BRA_pl_PSP_supporters_derived = BRA_pl_psp_supporters_modifier }
	add_to_variable = { BRA_pl_PRP_supporters_derived = BRA_pl_prp_supporters_modifier }

	clamp_variable = { var = BRA_pl_PTB_supporters_derived min = 0 max = BRA_PTB_seats }
	clamp_variable = { var = BRA_pl_PSD_supporters_derived min = 0 max = BRA_PSD_seats }
	clamp_variable = { var = BRA_pl_UDN_supporters_derived min = 0 max = BRA_UDN_seats }
	clamp_variable = { var = BRA_pl_PSP_supporters_derived min = 0 max = BRA_PSP_seats }
	clamp_variable = { var = BRA_pl_PRP_supporters_derived min = 0 max = BRA_PRP_seats }

	clear_array = BRA_pl_supporter_pips

	set_variable = { BRA_pl_total_support = BRA_PL_PTB_supporters_derived }
	resize_array = { array = BRA_pl_supporter_pips size = BRA_pl_total_support value = 3 }
	add_to_variable = { BRA_pl_total_support = BRA_PL_PSD_supporters_derived }
	resize_array = { array = BRA_pl_supporter_pips size = BRA_pl_total_support value = 1 }
	add_to_variable = { BRA_pl_total_support = BRA_PL_UDN_supporters_derived }
	resize_array = { array = BRA_pl_supporter_pips size = BRA_pl_total_support value = 2 }
	add_to_variable = { BRA_pl_total_support = BRA_PL_PSP_supporters_derived }
	resize_array = { array = BRA_pl_supporter_pips size = BRA_pl_total_support value = 4 }
	add_to_variable = { BRA_pl_total_support = BRA_PL_PRP_supporters_derived }
	resize_array = { array = BRA_pl_supporter_pips size = BRA_pl_total_support value = 5 }

	set_variable = { BRA_pl_enough_support = 1 }
	set_variable = { BRA_pl_support_needed = 34 }
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				check_variable = { BRA_pl_current_bill_id = token:BRA_EDNA_REPEAL_OF_JAPANESE_IMMIGRATION_BAN }
				check_variable = { BRA_pl_current_bill_id = token:BRA_LACERDA_REPEAL_OF_JAPANESE_IMMIGRATION_BAN }
				check_variable = { BRA_pl_current_bill_id = token:BRA_5TH_REPUBLIC_CONSTITUTION }
			}
		}
		set_variable = { BRA_pl_support_needed = 45 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				var = BRA_pl_total_support
				value = BRA_pl_support_needed
				compare = greater_than_or_equals
			}
		}
		set_variable = { BRA_pl_enough_support = 2 }
	}
}

###############################################################
########            Lacerda Coup Mechanic              ########
###############################################################

BRA_update_lacerda_coup = {
	clamp_variable = { var = BRA_lacerda_mil_support min = 0 max = 10 }
	clamp_variable = { var = BRA_lacerda_usa_support min = 0 max = 10 }
	clamp_variable = { var = BRA_lacerda_voter_support min = 0 max = 10 }
	clamp_variable = { var = BRA_lacerda_govt_support min = 0 max = 10 }

	set_variable = { BRA_lacerda_total_support = BRA_lacerda_mil_support }
	add_to_variable = { BRA_lacerda_total_support = BRA_lacerda_usa_support }
	add_to_variable = { BRA_lacerda_total_support = BRA_lacerda_voter_support }
	add_to_variable = { BRA_lacerda_total_support = BRA_lacerda_govt_support }

	divide_variable = { BRA_lacerda_total_support = 40 }
	multiply_variable = { BRA_lacerda_total_support = 20 }
	round_variable = BRA_lacerda_total_support
}

BRA_init_lacerda_mechanic = {
	set_country_flag = BRA_lacerda_coup_category_allowed
	activate_mission = BRA_lacerda_timeout
	set_variable = { BRA_lacerda_mil_support = 2 }
	set_variable = { BRA_lacerda_usa_support = 0 }
	set_variable = { BRA_lacerda_voter_support = 3 }
	set_variable = { BRA_lacerda_govt_support = 0 }
	set_variable = { BRA_lacerda_mil_support_decs = 0 }
	set_variable = { BRA_lacerda_usa_support_decs = 0 }
	set_variable = { BRA_lacerda_voter_support_decs = 0 }
	set_variable = { BRA_lacerda_govt_support_decs = 0 }
	if = {
		limit = { has_idea = OFN_Independent_Member }
		add_to_variable = { BRA_lacerda_usa_support = 4 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = BRA_petrobras }
		add_to_variable = { BRA_lacerda_govt_support = 3 }
	}
	else = {
		add_to_variable = { BRA_lacerda_usa_support = 1 }
	}

	if = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = BRA_Lott_Econ_Sphere }
		add_to_variable = { BRA_lacerda_usa_support = 1 }
	}

	clr_country_flag = BRA_lacerda_coup_hardliners
	clr_country_flag = BRA_lacerda_coup_sorbonne
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { BRA_military_winning_faction = 3 } }
		set_country_flag = BRA_lacerda_coup_hardliners
		add_to_variable = { BRA_lacerda_mil_support = 4 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { BRA_military_winning_faction = 1 } }
		set_country_flag = BRA_lacerda_coup_sorbonne
		add_to_variable = { BRA_lacerda_mil_support = 2 }
	}

	clr_country_flag = BRA_lacerda_coup_close_race
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { BRA_pres_second = 3 } }
		set_temp_variable = { difference = BRA_pres_winner_pct }
		subtract_from_temp_variable = { difference = BRA_pres_second_pct }

		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { difference < 2 } }
			set_country_flag = BRA_lacerda_coup_close_race
			add_to_variable = { BRA_lacerda_voter_support = 2 }
		}
	}

	clr_country_flag = BRA_udn_dominance
	set_temp_variable = { total_support_senado = BRA_UDN_seats }
	add_to_temp_variable = { total_support_senado = BRA_PSP_seats }
	add_to_temp_variable = { total_support_senado = BRA_PRP_seats }
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { total_support_senado > 32 } }
		set_country_flag = BRA_udn_dominance
		add_to_variable = { BRA_lacerda_govt_support = 3 }
	}

	BRA_update_lacerda_coup = yes
}

BRA_coalition_partners_abandon_UDN = {
	custom_effect_tooltip = BRA_coalition_partners_abandon_UDN
	hidden_effect = {

		set_variable = { BRA_senate_major_party_align^PARTY_PDC = PARTY_PSP }
		set_variable = { BRA_senate_major_party_align^PARTY_PTN = PARTY_PTB }
		set_variable = { BRA_senate_major_party_align^PARTY_PR  = PARTY_PSD }
		set_variable = { BRA_senate_major_party_align^PARTY_PL  = PARTY_PSP }

		BRA_redraw_senate_diagram = yes
		BRA_senate_select_state = yes
	}
}

###############################################################
########            Kubitschek Goals Plan              ########
###############################################################

# The Goals Plan has some custom modifiers defined in `common\modifier_definitions\TNO_brazil.txt`
#
# BRA_gp_failure_penalty                                                       - Modifies the penalty to Optimism when a goal is failed
# BRA_gp_megaproject_bonus                                                     - Modifies the bonus to Optimism from finishing a megaproject
# BRA_gp_people/business/creditors_optimism_weekly                             - Weekly change in Optimism for each group
# BRA_gp_energy/education/healthcare/development/infrastructure_progress_bonus - Bonus/malus to goal progress in each area

BRA_init_goals_plan = {
	BRA_begin_appointment_phase = yes

	clear_array = BRA_gp_available_cd_members

	add_to_array = { BRA_gp_available_cd_members = 1 }
	add_to_array = { BRA_gp_available_cd_members = 0 }
	add_to_array = { BRA_gp_available_cd_members = 11 }
	add_to_array = { BRA_gp_available_cd_members = 8 }
	add_to_array = { BRA_gp_available_cd_members = 2 }
	add_to_array = { BRA_gp_available_cd_members = 5 }
	add_to_array = { BRA_gp_available_cd_members = 3 }
	add_to_array = { BRA_gp_available_cd_members = 7 }
	add_to_array = { BRA_gp_available_cd_members = 12 }
	add_to_array = { BRA_gp_available_cd_members = 4 }
	add_to_array = { BRA_gp_available_cd_members = 6 }
	add_to_array = { BRA_gp_available_cd_members = 9 }
	add_to_array = { BRA_gp_available_cd_members = 10 }

	clear_array = BRA_gp_ptb_cd_members

	add_to_array = { BRA_gp_ptb_cd_members = 2 }
	add_to_array = { BRA_gp_ptb_cd_members = 3 }
	add_to_array = { BRA_gp_ptb_cd_members = 9 }
	add_to_array = { BRA_gp_ptb_cd_members = 11 }

	clear_array = BRA_gp_psd_cd_members

	add_to_array = { BRA_gp_psd_cd_members = 4 }
	add_to_array = { BRA_gp_psd_cd_members = 10 }
	add_to_array = { BRA_gp_psd_cd_members = 12 }

	set_variable = { BRA_gp_energy_goal = 60 }
	set_variable = { BRA_gp_education_goal = 80 }
	set_variable = { BRA_gp_healthcare_goal = 40 }
	set_variable = { BRA_gp_development_goal = 20 }
	set_variable = { BRA_gp_infrastructure_goal = 100 }

	set_variable = { BRA_gp_energy_progress = 35 }
	set_variable = { BRA_gp_education_progress = 63 }
	set_variable = { BRA_gp_healthcare_progress = 12 }
	set_variable = { BRA_gp_development_progress = 48 }
	set_variable = { BRA_gp_infrastructure_progress = 52 }

	clear_array = BRA_gp_energy_factions
	clear_array = BRA_gp_education_factions
	clear_array = BRA_gp_healthcare_factions
	clear_array = BRA_gp_development_factions
	clear_array = BRA_gp_infrastructure_factions

	#add_to_array = { BRA_gp_energy_factions = 3 }

	add_to_array = { BRA_gp_infrastructure_factions = 1 }

	add_to_array = { BRA_gp_education_factions = 0 }
	add_to_array = { BRA_gp_development_factions = 2 }

	set_variable = { BRA_gp_people_optimism = 60 }
	set_variable = { BRA_gp_business_optimism = 40 }
	set_variable = { BRA_gp_creditors_optimism = 40 }


	clear_array = BRA_gp_energy_progress_c
	resize_array = { array = BRA_gp_energy_progress_c value = 0 size = 5 }
	set_variable = { BRA_gp_energy_progress_c^0 = 0 } # Other
	set_variable = { BRA_gp_energy_progress_c^1 = 10 } # Focuses
	set_variable = { BRA_gp_energy_progress_c^2 = 17 } # Decisions
	set_variable = { BRA_gp_energy_progress_c^3 = 0 } # Megaprojects
	set_variable = { BRA_gp_energy_progress_c^4 = 8 } # Buildings

	resize_array = { array = BRA_gp_education_progress_c value = 0 size = 7 }
	set_variable = { BRA_gp_education_progress_c^0 = 0 } # Other
	set_variable = { BRA_gp_education_progress_c^1 = 0 } # Focuses
	set_variable = { BRA_gp_education_progress_c^2 = 0 } # Decisions
	set_variable = { BRA_gp_education_progress_c^3 = 0 } # Megaprojects
	set_variable = { BRA_gp_education_progress_c^4 = 0 } # Buildings
	set_variable = { BRA_gp_education_progress_c^5 = 0 } # Policy Effectiveness
	set_variable = { BRA_gp_education_progress_c^6 = 0 } # Socdev

	resize_array = { array = BRA_gp_healthcare_progress_c value = 0 size = 6 }
	set_variable = { BRA_gp_healthcare_progress_c^0 = 0 } # Other
	set_variable = { BRA_gp_healthcare_progress_c^1 = 0 } # Focuses
	set_variable = { BRA_gp_healthcare_progress_c^2 = 0 } # Decisions
	set_variable = { BRA_gp_healthcare_progress_c^3 = 0 } # Megaprojects
	set_variable = { BRA_gp_healthcare_progress_c^4 = 0 } # Buildings
	set_variable = { BRA_gp_healthcare_progress_c^5 = 0 } # Policy Effectiveness

	resize_array = { array = BRA_gp_development_progress_c value = 0 size = 5 }
	set_variable = { BRA_gp_development_progress_c^0 = 0 } # Other
	set_variable = { BRA_gp_development_progress_c^1 = 0 } # Focuses
	set_variable = { BRA_gp_development_progress_c^2 = 0 } # Decisions
	set_variable = { BRA_gp_development_progress_c^3 = 0 } # Megaprojects
	set_variable = { BRA_gp_development_progress_c^4 = 0 } # Socdev

	resize_array = { array = BRA_gp_infrastructure_progress_c value = 0 size = 6 }
	set_variable = { BRA_gp_infrastructure_progress_c^0 = 0 } # Other
	set_variable = { BRA_gp_infrastructure_progress_c^1 = 0 } # Focuses
	set_variable = { BRA_gp_infrastructure_progress_c^2 = 0 } # Decisions
	set_variable = { BRA_gp_infrastructure_progress_c^3 = 0 } # Megaprojects
	set_variable = { BRA_gp_infrastructure_progress_c^4 = 0 } # Buildings
	set_variable = { BRA_gp_infrastructure_progress_c^5 = 0 } # Socdev
}


BRA_open_jk_subtree = {
	custom_effect_tooltip = BRA_open_jk_subtree_tt
	add_to_variable = { BRA_gp_active_subtrees = 1 }
}
BRA_close_jk_subtree = {
	custom_effect_tooltip = BRA_close_jk_subtree_tt
	subtract_from_variable = { BRA_gp_active_subtrees = 1 }
	clamp_variable = {
		var = BRA_gp_active_subtrees
		min = 0
	}
}

BRA_begin_appointment_phase = {
	set_variable = { BRA_gp_phase = 1 }

	clear_array = BRA_gp_active_cd_members

	add_to_array = { BRA_gp_active_cd_members = -1 }
	add_to_array = { BRA_gp_active_cd_members = -1 }
	add_to_array = { BRA_gp_active_cd_members = -1 }
	add_to_array = { BRA_gp_active_cd_members = -1 }
	add_to_array = { BRA_gp_active_cd_members = -1 }

	set_variable = { BRA_gp_psd_points = 50 }

	BRA_set_up_goals_plan_timer = yes

	BRA_update_goals_plan_radar = yes

	country_event = {
		id = brazil_jk.10000
		days = 1
	}
}

BRA_begin_planning_phase = {
	set_variable = { BRA_gp_energy_goal = 40 }
	set_variable = { BRA_gp_education_goal = 40 }
	set_variable = { BRA_gp_healthcare_goal = 40 }
	set_variable = { BRA_gp_development_goal = 40 }
	set_variable = { BRA_gp_infrastructure_goal = 40 }

	BRA_recompute_weighted_goal_totals = yes

	set_variable = { BRA_gp_phase = 2 }

	set_variable = { BRA_gp_days_left_in_phase = 14 }
	BRA_update_goals_plan_timer = yes

	BRA_update_goals_plan_radar = yes

	country_event = {
		id = brazil_jk.10001
		days = 1
	}

	hidden_effect = {
		complete_national_focus = BRA_five_more_years
		complete_national_focus = BRA_assemble_development_council
	}
}

BRA_begin_execution_phase = {
	set_variable = { BRA_gp_phase = 3 }

	set_variable = { BRA_gp_days_left_in_phase = 337 }
	BRA_update_goals_plan_timer = yes

	BRA_update_goals_plan_radar = yes

	country_event = {
		id = brazil_jk.10003
		days = 7
	}

	hidden_effect = {
		complete_national_focus = BRA_announce_second_goals_plan
	}
}

BRA_set_goals = {
	set_variable = { BRA_gp_energy_goal = goal_num }
	set_variable = { BRA_gp_education_goal = goal_num }
	set_variable = { BRA_gp_healthcare_goal = goal_num }
	set_variable = { BRA_gp_development_goal = goal_num }
	set_variable = { BRA_gp_infrastructure_goal = goal_num }
	BRA_update_goals_plan_radar = yes
}
BRA_set_up_goals_plan_timer = {
	set_variable = { BRA_gp_days_left_in_phase = 14 }
	set_variable = { BRA_gp_phase_left_display = 100 }
}

BRA_update_goals_plan_timer = {
	set_temp_variable = { BRA_gp_timer_progress_temp = BRA_gp_days_left_in_phase }
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { BRA_gp_phase = 3 }
		}
		divide_temp_variable = { BRA_gp_timer_progress_temp = 337 }
	}
	else = {
		divide_temp_variable = { BRA_gp_timer_progress_temp = 14 }
	}
	multiply_temp_variable = { BRA_gp_timer_progress_temp = 100 }
	set_variable = { BRA_gp_phase_left_display = BRA_gp_timer_progress_temp }
}



BRA_add_cd_member = {
	BRA = {
		meta_effect = {
			text = {
				add_ideas = { BRA_gp_cd_member_[MEMBER_ID] }
			}
			MEMBER_ID = "[?added_member]"
		}
		force_update_dynamic_modifier = yes
	}
}

BRA_remove_cd_member = {
	BRA = {
		meta_effect = {
			text = {
				remove_ideas = { BRA_gp_cd_member_[MEMBER_ID] }
			}
			MEMBER_ID = "[?removed_member]"
		}
		force_update_dynamic_modifier = yes
	}
}


BRA_compute_psd_cd_members_point = {
	if = {#In case that there's no member in the CD
		limit = {
			find_highest_in_array = {
				array = BRA_gp_active_cd_members
				value = v
			}
			check_variable = { v = -1 }
		}
		set_variable = { BRA_gp_psd_points = 50 }
	}
	else = {
		set_temp_variable = { BRA_gp_psd_points_temp = 0 }
		set_temp_variable = { BRA_gp_psd_points_divisor = 5 }
		for_each_loop = {#Compute the divisor
			array = BRA_gp_active_cd_members

			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { v = -1 }
				}
				subtract_from_temp_variable = { BRA_gp_psd_points_divisor = 1 }
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { BRA_gp_psd_addend = 100 }
		set_temp_variable = { BRA_gp_neutral_addend = 50 }
		divide_temp_variable = { BRA_gp_psd_addend = BRA_gp_psd_points_divisor }
		divide_temp_variable = { BRA_gp_neutral_addend = BRA_gp_psd_points_divisor }
		for_each_loop = {
			array = BRA_gp_active_cd_members

			if = {
				limit = {
					is_in_array = {
						array = BRA_gp_psd_cd_members
						value = v
					}
				}
				add_to_temp_variable = { BRA_gp_psd_points_temp = BRA_gp_psd_addend }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						OR = {
							is_in_array = {
								array = BRA_gp_ptb_cd_members
								value = v
							}
							check_variable = { v = -1 }
						}
					}
					add_to_temp_variable = { BRA_gp_psd_points_temp = BRA_gp_neutral_addend }
				}
			}
		}
		set_variable = { BRA_gp_psd_points = BRA_gp_psd_points_temp }
	}
}



# Recomputes the weighted goal totals used for Optimism bonuses
BRA_recompute_weighted_goal_totals = {
	clear_array = BRA_gp_weighted_goal_totals
	add_to_array = { BRA_gp_weighted_goal_totals = 0 }
	add_to_array = { BRA_gp_weighted_goal_totals = 0 }
	add_to_array = { BRA_gp_weighted_goal_totals = 0 }

	# Use a meta-effect
	# Iterate over each target category to compute the weighted total of all goals
	# This is then multiplied to produce the bonuses for setting targets, meeting targets, and failing to meet targets

	for_loop_effect = {
		start = 0
		end = 5
		value = t_idx

		meta_effect = {
			text = {
				clear_array = BRA_gp_[TARGET_NAME]_weighted_goal_totals

				# Iterate over each group (people, business, creditors)
				for_loop_effect = {
					start = 0
					end = 3
					value = g_idx

					set_temp_variable = { base_bonus = BRA_gp_[TARGET_NAME]_goal }
					# If this group prioritizes this goal, double the weight
					if = {
						limit = { is_in_array = { BRA_gp_[TARGET_NAME]_factions = g_idx } }
						add_to_temp_variable = { base_bonus = BRA_gp_[TARGET_NAME]_goal }
					}
					add_to_array = { BRA_gp_[TARGET_NAME]_weighted_goal_totals = base_bonus }
					add_to_variable = { BRA_gp_weighted_goal_totals^g_idx = base_bonus }
				}
			}
			TARGET_NAME = "[BRA_gp_target_from_index]"
		}
	}

	BRA_recompute_bonuses = yes
}


# Recomputes the Optimism bonuses
# Requires that BRA_recompute_weighted_goal_totals is run after the last time that goals were changed
# In the execution phase then, you need only run this scripted effect
BRA_recompute_bonuses = {
	# Goal-setting bonuses
	set_variable = { BRA_gp_people_optimism_promise_bonus = BRA_gp_weighted_goal_totals^0 }
	set_variable = { BRA_gp_business_optimism_promise_bonus = BRA_gp_weighted_goal_totals^1 }
	set_variable = { BRA_gp_creditors_optimism_promise_bonus = BRA_gp_weighted_goal_totals^2 }
	multiply_variable = { BRA_gp_people_optimism_promise_bonus = 0.01 }
	multiply_variable = { BRA_gp_business_optimism_promise_bonus = 0.01 }
	multiply_variable = { BRA_gp_creditors_optimism_promise_bonus = 0.01 }

	set_variable = { BRA_gp_people_potential_optimism = BRA_gp_people_optimism }
	set_variable = { BRA_gp_business_potential_optimism = BRA_gp_business_optimism }
	set_variable = { BRA_gp_creditors_potential_optimism = BRA_gp_creditors_optimism }

	add_to_variable = { BRA_gp_people_potential_optimism = BRA_gp_people_optimism_promise_bonus }
	add_to_variable = { BRA_gp_business_potential_optimism = BRA_gp_business_optimism_promise_bonus }
	add_to_variable = { BRA_gp_creditors_potential_optimism = BRA_gp_creditors_optimism_promise_bonus }


	# Goal success bonuses
	set_variable = { BRA_gp_people_optimism_success_bonus = BRA_gp_weighted_goal_totals^0 }
	set_variable = { BRA_gp_business_optimism_success_bonus = BRA_gp_weighted_goal_totals^1 }
	set_variable = { BRA_gp_creditors_optimism_success_bonus = BRA_gp_weighted_goal_totals^2 }
	multiply_variable = { BRA_gp_people_optimism_success_bonus = 0.04 }
	multiply_variable = { BRA_gp_business_optimism_success_bonus = 0.04 }
	multiply_variable = { BRA_gp_creditors_optimism_success_bonus = 0.04 }

	# Goal failure bonus
	set_variable = { BRA_gp_people_optimism_failure_bonus = BRA_gp_weighted_goal_totals^0 }
	set_variable = { BRA_gp_business_optimism_failure_bonus = BRA_gp_weighted_goal_totals^1 }
	set_variable = { BRA_gp_creditors_optimism_failure_bonus = BRA_gp_weighted_goal_totals^2 }
	multiply_variable = { BRA_gp_people_optimism_failure_bonus = -0.04 }
	multiply_variable = { BRA_gp_business_optimism_failure_bonus = -0.04 }
	multiply_variable = { BRA_gp_creditors_optimism_failure_bonus = -0.04 }

	for_loop_effect = {
		start = 0
		end = 5
		value = t_idx

		meta_effect = {
			text = {
				set_variable = { BRA_gp_[TARGET_NAME]_people_optimism_success_bonus = BRA_gp_[TARGET_NAME]_weighted_goal_totals^0 }
				set_variable = { BRA_gp_[TARGET_NAME]_business_optimism_success_bonus = BRA_gp_[TARGET_NAME]_weighted_goal_totals^1 }
				set_variable = { BRA_gp_[TARGET_NAME]_creditors_optimism_success_bonus = BRA_gp_[TARGET_NAME]_weighted_goal_totals^2 }
				multiply_variable = { BRA_gp_[TARGET_NAME]_people_optimism_success_bonus = 0.04 }
				multiply_variable = { BRA_gp_[TARGET_NAME]_business_optimism_success_bonus = 0.04 }
				multiply_variable = { BRA_gp_[TARGET_NAME]_creditors_optimism_success_bonus = 0.04 }


				set_variable = { BRA_gp_[TARGET_NAME]_people_optimism_failure_bonus = BRA_gp_[TARGET_NAME]_weighted_goal_totals^0 }
				set_variable = { BRA_gp_[TARGET_NAME]_business_optimism_failure_bonus = BRA_gp_[TARGET_NAME]_weighted_goal_totals^1 }
				set_variable = { BRA_gp_[TARGET_NAME]_creditors_optimism_failure_bonus = BRA_gp_[TARGET_NAME]_weighted_goal_totals^2 }
				multiply_variable = { BRA_gp_[TARGET_NAME]_people_optimism_failure_bonus = -0.04 }
				multiply_variable = { BRA_gp_[TARGET_NAME]_business_optimism_failure_bonus = -0.04 }
				multiply_variable = { BRA_gp_[TARGET_NAME]_creditors_optimism_failure_bonus = -0.04 }
			}
			TARGET_NAME = "[BRA_gp_target_from_index]"
		}
	}
}

BRA_gp_end_of_year_speech = {
	set_variable = { BRA_gp_people_optimism_actual_bonus = 0 }
	set_variable = { BRA_gp_business_optimism_actual_bonus = 0 }
	set_variable = { BRA_gp_creditors_optimism_actual_bonus = 0 }

	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { BRA_gp_energy_progress < BRA_gp_energy_goal } }
		add_to_variable = { BRA_gp_people_optimism_actual_bonus = BRA_gp_energy_people_optimism_failure_bonus }
		add_to_variable = { BRA_gp_business_optimism_actual_bonus = BRA_gp_energy_business_optimism_failure_bonus }
		add_to_variable = { BRA_gp_creditors_optimism_actual_bonus = BRA_gp_energy_creditors_optimism_failure_bonus }
	} else = {
		add_to_variable = { BRA_gp_people_optimism_actual_bonus = BRA_gp_energy_people_optimism_success_bonus }
		add_to_variable = { BRA_gp_business_optimism_actual_bonus = BRA_gp_energy_business_optimism_success_bonus }
		add_to_variable = { BRA_gp_creditors_optimism_actual_bonus = BRA_gp_energy_creditors_optimism_success_bonus }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { BRA_gp_education_progress < BRA_gp_education_goal } }
		add_to_variable = { BRA_gp_people_optimism_actual_bonus = BRA_gp_education_people_optimism_failure_bonus }
		add_to_variable = { BRA_gp_business_optimism_actual_bonus = BRA_gp_education_business_optimism_failure_bonus }
		add_to_variable = { BRA_gp_creditors_optimism_actual_bonus = BRA_gp_education_creditors_optimism_failure_bonus }
	} else = {
		add_to_variable = { BRA_gp_people_optimism_actual_bonus = BRA_gp_education_people_optimism_success_bonus }
		add_to_variable = { BRA_gp_business_optimism_actual_bonus = BRA_gp_education_business_optimism_success_bonus }
		add_to_variable = { BRA_gp_creditors_optimism_actual_bonus = BRA_gp_education_creditors_optimism_success_bonus }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { BRA_gp_healthcare_progress < BRA_gp_healthcare_goal } }
		add_to_variable = { BRA_gp_people_optimism_actual_bonus = BRA_gp_healthcare_people_optimism_failure_bonus }
		add_to_variable = { BRA_gp_business_optimism_actual_bonus = BRA_gp_healthcare_business_optimism_failure_bonus }
		add_to_variable = { BRA_gp_creditors_optimism_actual_bonus = BRA_gp_healthcare_creditors_optimism_failure_bonus }
	} else = {
		add_to_variable = { BRA_gp_people_optimism_actual_bonus = BRA_gp_healthcare_people_optimism_success_bonus }
		add_to_variable = { BRA_gp_business_optimism_actual_bonus = BRA_gp_healthcare_business_optimism_success_bonus }
		add_to_variable = { BRA_gp_creditors_optimism_actual_bonus = BRA_gp_healthcare_creditors_optimism_success_bonus }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { BRA_gp_development_progress < BRA_gp_development_goal } }
		add_to_variable = { BRA_gp_people_optimism_actual_bonus = BRA_gp_development_people_optimism_failure_bonus }
		add_to_variable = { BRA_gp_business_optimism_actual_bonus = BRA_gp_development_business_optimism_failure_bonus }
		add_to_variable = { BRA_gp_creditors_optimism_actual_bonus = BRA_gp_development_creditors_optimism_failure_bonus }
	} else = {
		add_to_variable = { BRA_gp_people_optimism_actual_bonus = BRA_gp_development_people_optimism_success_bonus }
		add_to_variable = { BRA_gp_business_optimism_actual_bonus = BRA_gp_development_business_optimism_success_bonus }
		add_to_variable = { BRA_gp_creditors_optimism_actual_bonus = BRA_gp_development_creditors_optimism_success_bonus }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { BRA_gp_infrastructure_progress < BRA_gp_infrastructure_goal } }
		add_to_variable = { BRA_gp_people_optimism_actual_bonus = BRA_gp_infrastructure_people_optimism_failure_bonus }
		add_to_variable = { BRA_gp_business_optimism_actual_bonus = BRA_gp_infrastructure_business_optimism_failure_bonus }
		add_to_variable = { BRA_gp_creditors_optimism_actual_bonus = BRA_gp_infrastructure_creditors_optimism_failure_bonus }
	} else = {
		add_to_variable = { BRA_gp_people_optimism_actual_bonus = BRA_gp_infrastructure_people_optimism_success_bonus }
		add_to_variable = { BRA_gp_business_optimism_actual_bonus = BRA_gp_infrastructure_business_optimism_success_bonus }
		add_to_variable = { BRA_gp_creditors_optimism_actual_bonus = BRA_gp_infrastructure_creditors_optimism_success_bonus }
	}
}

BRA_process_goals_end_of_year = {
	custom_effect_tooltip = BRA_gp_optimism_change_header
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { BRA_gp_energy_progress < BRA_gp_energy_goal } }
		custom_effect_tooltip = BRA_gp_energy_failure_tt
		set_temp_variable = { people_display = BRA_gp_energy_people_optimism_failure_bonus }
		set_temp_variable = { business_display = BRA_gp_energy_business_optimism_failure_bonus }
		set_temp_variable = { creditors_display = BRA_gp_energy_creditors_optimism_failure_bonus }

	} else = {
		custom_effect_tooltip = BRA_gp_energy_success_tt

		set_temp_variable = { business_display = BRA_gp_energy_business_optimism_success_bonus }
		set_temp_variable = { creditors_display = BRA_gp_energy_creditors_optimism_success_bonus }

		set_temp_variable = { people_display = BRA_gp_development_people_optimism_failure_bonus }
		set_temp_variable = { business_display = BRA_gp_development_business_optimism_failure_bonus }
		set_temp_variable = { creditors_display = BRA_gp_development_creditors_optimism_failure_bonus }

		set_temp_variable = { people_display = BRA_gp_development_people_optimism_success_bonus }
		set_temp_variable = { business_display = BRA_gp_development_business_optimism_success_bonus }
		set_temp_variable = { creditors_display = BRA_gp_development_creditors_optimism_success_bonus }

}

BRA_compact_optimism_change = { # I swear I didn't copy anything
	add_to_variable = { BRA_gp_people_optimism = people_display }
	add_to_variable = { BRA_gp_business_optimism = business_display }
	add_to_variable = { BRA_gp_creditors_optimism = creditors_display }
	custom_effect_tooltip = BRA_optimism_change_tt
	clamp_variable = {
		var = BRA_gp_people_optimism
		min = 0
		max = 100
	}
	clamp_variable = {
		var = BRA_gp_business_optimism
		min = 0
		max = 100
	}
	clamp_variable = {
		var = BRA_gp_creditors_optimism
		min = 0
		max = 100
	}
}

BRA_align_goals_plan_counters = {
	set_variable = { BRA_gp_last_total_hospitals = total_hospitals }
	set_variable = { BRA_gp_last_total_schools = total_schools }
	set_variable = { BRA_gp_last_total_thermo = total_thermo_plants }

	set_variable = { BRA_gp_last_total_infra = total_infrastructure }
	set_variable = { BRA_gp_last_total_air = total_air_bases }
	set_variable = { BRA_gp_last_total_naval = total_naval_bases }
}

BRA_goals_plan_weekly = {
	clear_variable = total_infrastructure
	clear_variable = total_air_bases
	clear_variable = total_naval_bases
	every_owned_state = {
		add_to_variable = { PREV.total_infrastructure = non_damaged_building_level@infrastructure }
		add_to_variable = { PREV.total_air_bases = non_damaged_building_level@air_base }
		add_to_variable = { PREV.total_naval_bases = non_damaged_building_level@naval_base }
	}


	# Healthcare bonus from hospitals
	set_temp_variable = { hospitals_difference = total_hospitals }
	subtract_from_temp_variable = { hospitals_difference = BRA_gp_last_total_hospitals }

	set_temp_variable = { temp_progress = hospitals_difference }
	multiply_temp_variable = { temp_progress = 4 }
	set_temp_variable = { temp_category = 4 }
	BRA_gp_add_healthcare_progress = yes

	# Education bonus from schools
	set_temp_variable = { schools_difference = total_schools }
	subtract_from_temp_variable = { schools_difference = BRA_gp_last_total_schools }

	set_temp_variable = { temp_progress = schools_difference }
	multiply_temp_variable = { temp_progress = 2 }
	set_temp_variable = { temp_category = 4 }
	BRA_gp_add_education_progress = yes


	# Energy bonus from thermo plants
	set_temp_variable = { thermos_difference = total_thermo_plants }
	subtract_from_temp_variable = { thermos_difference = BRA_gp_last_total_thermo }

	set_temp_variable = { temp_progress = thermos_difference }
	multiply_temp_variable = { temp_progress = 3 }
	set_temp_variable = { temp_category = 4 }
	BRA_gp_add_energy_progress = yes

	# Infra bonus from various buildings
	set_temp_variable = { infrastructure_difference = total_infrastructure }
	subtract_from_temp_variable = { infrastructure_difference = BRA_gp_last_total_infra }
	set_temp_variable = { air_bases_difference = total_air_bases }
	subtract_from_temp_variable = { air_bases_difference = BRA_gp_last_total_air }
	set_temp_variable = { naval_bases_difference = total_naval_bases }
	subtract_from_temp_variable = { naval_bases_difference = BRA_gp_last_total_naval }

	set_temp_variable = { temp_progress = thermos_difference }
	add_to_temp_variable = { temp_progress = air_bases_difference }
	add_to_temp_variable = { temp_progress = naval_bases_difference }
	add_to_temp_variable = { temp_progress = naval_bases_difference }

	set_temp_variable = { temp_category = 4 }
	BRA_gp_add_infrastructure_progress = yes

	BRA_align_goals_plan_counters = yes


	# Weekly Education bonus from policy effectiveness
	set_temp_variable = { temp_progress = tno_education_effectiveness_actual }
	divide_temp_variable = { temp_progress = 100 }
	set_temp_variable = { temp_category = 5 }
	BRA_gp_add_education_progress = yes

	# Weekly Healthcare bonus from policy effectiveness
	set_temp_variable = { temp_progress = tno_health_care_effectiveness_actual }
	divide_temp_variable = { temp_progress = 100 }
	set_temp_variable = { temp_category = 5 }
	BRA_gp_add_healthcare_progress = yes

}




BRA_gp_add_energy_progress = {
	set_temp_variable = { modified_temp_progress = 1 }
	add_to_temp_variable = { modified_temp_progress = modifier@BRA_gp_energy_progress_bonus }
	multiply_temp_variable = { modified_temp_progress = temp_progress }

	add_to_variable = { BRA_gp_energy_progress = modified_temp_progress }
	custom_effect_tooltip = BRA_gp_energy_progress_increase_tt

	clamp_variable = { var = BRA_gp_energy_progress min = 0 max = 100 }

	add_to_variable = { BRA_gp_energy_progress_c^temp_category = modified_temp_progress }
	BRA_update_goals_plan_radar = yes
}
BRA_gp_add_energy_progress_focus = {
	set_temp_variable = { temp_category = 1 }
	BRA_gp_add_energy_progress = yes
}
BRA_gp_add_energy_progress_decision = {
	set_temp_variable = { temp_category = 2 }
	BRA_gp_add_energy_progress = yes
}
BRA_gp_add_energy_progress_project = {
	set_temp_variable = { temp_category = 3 }
	BRA_gp_add_energy_progress = yes
}

BRA_gp_add_healthcare_progress = {
	set_temp_variable = { modified_temp_progress = 1 }
	add_to_temp_variable = { modified_temp_progress = modifier@BRA_gp_healthcare_progress_bonus }
	multiply_temp_variable = { modified_temp_progress = temp_progress }

	add_to_variable = { BRA_gp_healthcare_progress = modified_temp_progress }
	custom_effect_tooltip = BRA_gp_healthcare_progress_increase_tt

	clamp_variable = { var = BRA_gp_healthcare_progress min = 0 max = 100 }

	add_to_variable = { BRA_gp_healthcare_progress_c^temp_category = modified_temp_progress }
	BRA_update_goals_plan_radar = yes
}
BRA_gp_add_healthcare_progress_focus = {
	set_temp_variable = { temp_category = 1 }
	BRA_gp_add_healthcare_progress = yes
}
BRA_gp_add_healthcare_progress_decision = {
	set_temp_variable = { temp_category = 2 }
	BRA_gp_add_healthcare_progress = yes
}
BRA_gp_add_healthcare_progress_project = {
	set_temp_variable = { temp_category = 3 }
	BRA_gp_add_healthcare_progress = yes
}

BRA_gp_add_infrastructure_progress = {
	set_temp_variable = { modified_temp_progress = 1 }
	add_to_temp_variable = { modified_temp_progress = modifier@BRA_gp_infrastructure_progress_bonus }
	multiply_temp_variable = { modified_temp_progress = temp_progress }

	add_to_variable = { BRA_gp_infrastructure_progress = modified_temp_progress }
	custom_effect_tooltip = BRA_gp_infrastructure_progress_increase_tt

	clamp_variable = { var = BRA_gp_infrastructure_progress min = 0 max = 100 }

	add_to_variable = { BRA_gp_infrastructure_progress_c^temp_category = modified_temp_progress }
	BRA_update_goals_plan_radar = yes
}

BRA_update_goals_plan_radar = {
	set_variable = { BRA_gp_radar_goal_0 = BRA_gp_energy_goal }
	round_variable = BRA_gp_radar_goal_0
	multiply_variable = { BRA_gp_radar_goal_0 = 1000 }
	add_to_variable = { BRA_gp_radar_goal_0 = BRA_gp_education_goal }
	round_variable = BRA_gp_radar_goal_0


	set_variable = { BRA_gp_radar_goal_1 = BRA_gp_education_goal }
	round_variable = BRA_gp_radar_goal_1
	multiply_variable = { BRA_gp_radar_goal_1 = 1000 }
	add_to_variable = { BRA_gp_radar_goal_1 = BRA_gp_healthcare_goal }
	round_variable = BRA_gp_radar_goal_1


	set_variable = { BRA_gp_radar_goal_2 = BRA_gp_healthcare_goal }
	round_variable = BRA_gp_radar_goal_2
	multiply_variable = { BRA_gp_radar_goal_2 = 1000 }
	add_to_variable = { BRA_gp_radar_goal_2 = BRA_gp_development_goal }
	round_variable = BRA_gp_radar_goal_2


	set_variable = { BRA_gp_radar_goal_3 = BRA_gp_development_goal }
	round_variable = BRA_gp_radar_goal_3
	multiply_variable = { BRA_gp_radar_goal_3 = 1000 }
	add_to_variable = { BRA_gp_radar_goal_3 = BRA_gp_infrastructure_goal }
	round_variable = BRA_gp_radar_goal_3


	set_variable = { BRA_gp_radar_goal_4 = BRA_gp_infrastructure_goal }
	round_variable = BRA_gp_radar_goal_4
	multiply_variable = { BRA_gp_radar_goal_4 = 1000 }
	add_to_variable = { BRA_gp_radar_goal_4 = BRA_gp_energy_goal }
	round_variable = BRA_gp_radar_goal_4


	set_variable = { BRA_gp_radar_progress_0 = BRA_gp_energy_progress }
	round_variable = BRA_gp_radar_progress_0
	multiply_variable = { BRA_gp_radar_progress_0 = 1000 }
	add_to_variable = { BRA_gp_radar_progress_0 = BRA_gp_education_progress }
	round_variable = BRA_gp_radar_progress_0


	set_variable = { BRA_gp_radar_progress_1 = BRA_gp_education_progress }
	round_variable = BRA_gp_radar_progress_1
	multiply_variable = { BRA_gp_radar_progress_1 = 1000 }
	add_to_variable = { BRA_gp_radar_progress_1 = BRA_gp_healthcare_progress }
	round_variable = BRA_gp_radar_progress_1


	set_variable = { BRA_gp_radar_progress_2 = BRA_gp_healthcare_progress }
	round_variable = BRA_gp_radar_progress_2
	multiply_variable = { BRA_gp_radar_progress_2 = 1000 }
	add_to_variable = { BRA_gp_radar_progress_2 = BRA_gp_development_progress }
	round_variable = BRA_gp_radar_progress_2


	set_variable = { BRA_gp_radar_progress_3 = BRA_gp_development_progress }
	round_variable = BRA_gp_radar_progress_3
	multiply_variable = { BRA_gp_radar_progress_3 = 1000 }
	add_to_variable = { BRA_gp_radar_progress_3 = BRA_gp_infrastructure_progress }
	round_variable = BRA_gp_radar_progress_3


	set_variable = { BRA_gp_radar_progress_4 = BRA_gp_infrastructure_progress }
	round_variable = BRA_gp_radar_progress_4
	multiply_variable = { BRA_gp_radar_progress_4 = 1000 }
	add_to_variable = { BRA_gp_radar_progress_4 = BRA_gp_energy_progress }
	round_variable = BRA_gp_radar_progress_4
}

BRA_trigger_military_coup = {
	hidden_effect = {
		set_cosmetic_tag = BRA_military_coup
		remove_ideas = BRA_hundred_days
		remove_ideas = BRA_overbearing_military
		add_ideas = BRA_death_of_the_dream
		add_ideas = BRA_day_of_the_jackboot
	}
	log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Coup firing"
	set_country_flag = BRA_military_coup_happened
	set_country_flag = BRA_military_dictatorship
	clr_country_flag = BRA_military_coup_scheduled

	clr_country_flag = BRA_lottquadros_category_allowed

	add_stability = -0.3

	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { stability < 0 } }
		set_stability = 0
	}

	add_popularity = {
		ideology = despotism
		popularity = 0.3
	}
	add_popularity = {
		ideology = socialist
		popularity = -0.05
	}
	add_popularity = {
		ideology = communist
		popularity = 0.05
	}
	set_politics = {
		ruling_party = despotism
		elections_allowed = no
	}
	add_country_leader_role = {
		character = BRA_Ranieri_Mazzilli
		promote_leader = yes
		country_leader = {
			desc = "POLITICS_RANIERI_MAZZILLI_DESC"
			expire = "1994.4.20"
			ideology = despotism_interim_government_subtype
			traits = { }
			id = -1
		}
	}
	load_focus_tree = {
		tree = BRA_HundredDays_MilitaryCoup_tree
		keep_completed = no
	}
	add_ideas = BRA_idea_nationwide_chaos_max
	custom_effect_tooltip = BRA_new_cabinet_tt
	hidden_effect = {
		remove_ideas = {
			BRA_Humberto_Castelo_Branco_high_command
			BRA_Silvio_Heck_navy_chief
		}
		add_ideas = {
			BRA_Amaury_Kruel_high_command
			BRA_Augusto_Rademaker_navy_chief
		}
		remove_all_ministers = yes
		add_ideas = {
			BRA_Auro_de_Moura_Andrade_hog
			BRA_Juracy_Magalhaes_for
			BRA_Delfim_Netto_eco
			BRA_Costa_e_Silva_sec
		}
	}
	clr_country_flag = BRA_hundred_days_category_allowed
	BRA_dissolve_the_senate = yes
}

BRA_initialize_military = {
	# 23% for Hardline, 46 % for Sorbonne, 31% for Constitutionalists
	set_variable = { BRA_military_hardliners_power = 23 }
	set_variable = { BRA_military_sorbonne_power = 46 }
	set_variable = { BRA_military_const_power = 31 }
	set_variable = { BRA_military_progressistas_power = 0 }

	set_variable = { BRA_military_nepotism = 35 }
	set_variable = { BRA_military_loyalty = 55 }
	set_variable = { BRA_nepotism_variable = 0 }

	BRA_military_update = yes
}

BRA_military_update = {
	clamp_variable = { var = BRA_military_nepotism min = 0 max = 100 }
	clamp_variable = { var = BRA_military_loyalty min = 0 max = 100 }
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { BRA_military_nepotism > 83.33 } }
		add_ideas = { BRA_army_nepotism_6 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { BRA_military_nepotism > 66.66 } }
		add_ideas = { BRA_army_nepotism_5 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { BRA_military_nepotism > 50 } }
		add_ideas = { BRA_army_nepotism_4 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { BRA_military_nepotism > 33.33 } }
		add_ideas = { BRA_army_nepotism_3 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { BRA_military_nepotism > 16.66 } }
		add_ideas = { BRA_army_nepotism_2 }
	}
	else = {
		add_ideas = { BRA_army_nepotism_1 }
	}

	BRA_military_normalize_power = yes
	BRA_military_update_factions = yes
}

BRA_military_normalize_power = {
	clamp_variable = { var = BRA_military_hardliners_power min = 0 max = 100 }
	clamp_variable = { var = BRA_military_sorbonne_power min = 0 max = 100 }
	clamp_variable = { var = BRA_military_const_power min = 0 max = 100 }
	clamp_variable = { var = BRA_military_progressistas_power min = 0 max = 100 }

	set_temp_variable = { total = BRA_military_hardliners_power }
	add_to_temp_variable = { total = BRA_military_sorbonne_power }
	add_to_temp_variable = { total = BRA_military_const_power }
	add_to_temp_variable = { total = BRA_military_progressistas_power }

	set_temp_variable = { mult = 100 }
	divide_temp_variable = { mult = total }
	multiply_variable = { BRA_military_const_power = mult }
	multiply_variable = { BRA_military_sorbonne_power = mult }
	multiply_variable = { BRA_military_hardliners_power = mult }
	multiply_variable = { BRA_military_progressistas_power = mult }
}

BRA_military_update_factions = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			AND = {
				check_variable = { BRA_military_hardliners_power > BRA_military_sorbonne_power }
				check_variable = { BRA_military_hardliners_power > BRA_military_const_power }
				check_variable = { BRA_military_hardliners_power > BRA_military_progressistas_power }
			}
		}
		set_variable = { BRA_military_winning_faction = 3 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			AND = {
				check_variable = { BRA_military_sorbonne_power > BRA_military_hardliners_power }
				check_variable = { BRA_military_sorbonne_power > BRA_military_const_power }
				check_variable = { BRA_military_sorbonne_power > BRA_military_progressistas_power }
			}
		}
		set_variable = { BRA_military_winning_faction = 1 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			AND = {
				check_variable = { BRA_military_const_power > BRA_military_hardliners_power }
				check_variable = { BRA_military_const_power > BRA_military_sorbonne_power }
				check_variable = { BRA_military_const_power > BRA_military_progressistas_power }
			}
		}
		set_variable = { BRA_military_winning_faction = 2 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			AND = {
				check_variable = { BRA_military_progressistas_power > BRA_military_hardliners_power }
				check_variable = { BRA_military_progressistas_power > BRA_military_sorbonne_power }
				check_variable = { BRA_military_progressistas_power > BRA_military_const_power }
			}
		}
		set_variable = { BRA_military_winning_faction = 4 }
	}
	else = {
		set_variable = { BRA_military_winning_faction = 5 } # No dominant faction
	}
}

BRA_nepotism_check = {
	if = {
		limit = { has_idea = BRA_army_nepotism_5 }
		set_variable = { BRA_nepotism_variable = 3 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_idea = BRA_army_nepotism_4 }
		set_variable = { BRA_nepotism_variable = 2 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_idea = BRA_army_nepotism_3 }
		set_variable = { BRA_nepotism_variable = 1 }
	}
	else = {
		set_variable = { BRA_nepotism_variable = 0 }
	}
}

BRA_loyalty_monthly = {
	subtract_from_variable = { BRA_military_loyalty = 1 }
}

	hidden_effect = {

		add_to_variable = { BRA_military_hardliners_power = 2.5 }
		add_to_variable = { BRA_military_const_power = 2.5 }
		BRA_military_update = yes
	}
}

	add_to_array = { BRA_develop_region_pop = population }
	add_to_temp_array = { value_diffs = population }

	multiply_temp_variable = { value_diffs^0 = 0.01 }
	multiply_temp_variable = { value_diffs^1 = 0.01 }
	multiply_temp_variable = { value_diffs^2 = 0.01 }
	multiply_temp_variable = { value_diffs^3 = 0.01 }
	multiply_temp_variable = { value_diffs^4 = 0.01 }

	clear_array = BRA_develop_region_pop_history
	for_loop_effect = {
		start = 0
		end = 5
		value = j

		set_temp_variable = { k = 4 }
		subtract_from_temp_variable = { k = j }

		set_temp_variable = { current = BRA_develop_region_pop^k }
		set_temp_variable = { diff = value_diffs^k }
		divide_temp_variable = { diff = 12 }

		for_loop_effect = {
			start = 0
			end = 13
			value = i

			add_to_array = { array = BRA_develop_region_pop_history value = current index = 0 }

			set_temp_variable = { r = random }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { r = 0.5 }
			multiply_temp_variable = { r = 0.8 }
			add_to_temp_variable = { r = 1.0 }
			multiply_temp_variable = { r = diff }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { current = r }
		}
	}

	clear_array = BRA_develop_region_urban_pop_trend

	add_to_array = { BRA_develop_region_urban_pop_trend = 3 }

	divide_variable = { BRA_develop_region_urban_pop_trend^1 = 12 }
	divide_variable = { BRA_develop_region_urban_pop_trend^2 = 12 }
	divide_variable = { BRA_develop_region_urban_pop_trend^3 = 12 }
	divide_variable = { BRA_develop_region_urban_pop_trend^4 = 12 }

		start = 0
		end = 13
		value = i

		add_to_array = { array = BRA_develop_pop_history value = current index = 0 }

	for_loop_effect = {
		start = 0
		end = 13
		value = i

		set_temp_variable = { current = 0 }
		set_temp_variable = { divisor = 0 }

		for_loop_effect = {
			start = 0
			end = 5
			value = j

			set_temp_variable = { base = j }
			multiply_temp_variable = { base = 13 }
			add_to_temp_variable = { base = i }

			set_temp_variable = { to_add = BRA_develop_region_industry_history^base }
			divide_temp_variable = { to_add = 100 }
			multiply_temp_variable = { to_add = BRA_develop_region_pop_history^base }
			add_to_temp_variable = { current = to_add }

			set_temp_variable = { pop_to_add = BRA_develop_region_pop_history^base }
			divide_temp_variable = { pop_to_add = 100 }
			add_to_temp_variable = { divisor = pop_to_add }
		}
		divide_temp_variable = { current = divisor }

		add_to_array = { array = BRA_develop_industry_pct_gdp_history value = current }
	}
	set_variable = { BRA_develop_industry_pct_gdp = BRA_develop_industry_pct_gdp_history^12 }


	BRA_develop_ready_graph =yes
}
