# Redraws a graph
# Called every month when numbers update and when the player chooses to view a different stat
BRA_develop_ready_graph = {
	# Update frames of buttons
	clear_array = BRA_develop_is_stat_selected
	resize_array = {
		array = BRA_develop_is_stat_selected
		value = 1
		size = 8
	}
	set_variable = { BRA_develop_is_stat_selected^BRA_develop_graph_selected_stat = 2 }

	# Fill graph values with appropriate values, based on selected stat
	# Here, BRA_develop_graph_base_unit is the base "unit", 0 is none, 1 is K, 2 is M, 3 is B, -1 is percentage
	clear_array = BRA_develop_graph_values
	clear_array = BRA_develop_graph_target_values
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { BRA_develop_graph_selected_stat = 0 }
		}
		set_variable = { BRA_develop_graph_base_unit = 2 }
		for_loop_effect = {
			start = 0
			end = 13
			value = i

			add_to_array = { BRA_develop_graph_values = BRA_develop_GDP_history^i }
			set_temp_variable = { holder = BRA_TargetGDPGrowth }
			multiply_temp_variable = { holder = 1000 }
			add_to_array = { BRA_develop_graph_target_values = holder }
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { BRA_develop_graph_selected_stat = 2 }
		}
		set_variable = { BRA_develop_graph_base_unit = -1 }
		for_loop_effect = {
			start = 0
			end = 13
			value = i

			add_to_array = { BRA_develop_graph_values = BRA_develop_inflation_history^i }
			add_to_array = { BRA_develop_graph_target_values = BRA_TargetInflation }
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { BRA_develop_graph_selected_stat = 1 }
		}
		set_variable = { BRA_develop_graph_base_unit = 1 }
		for_loop_effect = {
			start = 0
			end = 13
			value = i

			add_to_array = { BRA_develop_graph_values = BRA_develop_pop_history^i }
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { BRA_develop_graph_selected_stat = 3 }
		}
		set_variable = { BRA_develop_graph_base_unit = -1 }
		for_loop_effect = {
			start = 0
			end = 13
			value = i

			add_to_array = { BRA_develop_graph_values = BRA_develop_industry_pct_gdp_history^i }
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { BRA_develop_graph_selected_stat = 4 }
		}
		set_variable = { BRA_develop_graph_base_unit = 1 }

		set_temp_variable = { base = BRA_develop_selected_region }
		multiply_temp_variable = { base = 13 }

		for_loop_effect = {
			start = 0
			end = 13
			value = i

			set_temp_variable = { idx = i }
			add_to_temp_variable = { idx = base }
			add_to_array = { BRA_develop_graph_values = BRA_develop_region_pop_history^idx }
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { BRA_develop_graph_selected_stat = 5 }
		}
		set_variable = { BRA_develop_graph_base_unit = -1 }

		set_temp_variable = { base = BRA_develop_selected_region }
		multiply_temp_variable = { base = 13 }

		for_loop_effect = {
			start = 0
			end = 13
			value = i

			set_temp_variable = { idx = i }
			add_to_temp_variable = { idx = base }
			add_to_array = { BRA_develop_graph_values = BRA_develop_region_urban_pop_history^idx }
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { BRA_develop_graph_selected_stat = 6 }
		}
		set_variable = { BRA_develop_graph_base_unit = -1 }

		set_temp_variable = { base = BRA_develop_selected_region }
		multiply_temp_variable = { base = 13 }

		for_loop_effect = {
			start = 0
			end = 13
			value = i

			set_temp_variable = { idx = i }
			add_to_temp_variable = { idx = base }
			add_to_array = { BRA_develop_graph_values = BRA_develop_region_mech_rate_history^idx }
		}
	}
	else = {
		set_variable = { BRA_develop_graph_base_unit = -1 }

		set_temp_variable = { base = BRA_develop_selected_region }
		multiply_temp_variable = { base = 13 }

		for_loop_effect = {
			start = 0
			end = 13
			value = i

			set_temp_variable = { idx = i }
			add_to_temp_variable = { idx = base }
			add_to_array = { BRA_develop_graph_values = BRA_develop_region_industry_history^idx }
		}
	}

	clear_array = BRA_develop_graph_offsets
	clear_array = BRA_develop_graph_deltas
	clear_array = BRA_develop_graph_vbars
	clear_array = BRA_develop_graph_vbar_offsets
	clear_array = BRA_develop_graph_target_deltas
	clear_array = BRA_develop_graph_target_offsets

	# Find minimum and maximum values visible on graph
	set_temp_variable = { min = BRA_develop_graph_values^0 }
	set_temp_variable = { max = BRA_develop_graph_values^0 }
	for_loop_effect = {
		end = 13
		value = i

		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { BRA_develop_graph_values^i > max }
			}
			set_temp_variable = { max = BRA_develop_graph_values^i }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { BRA_develop_graph_values^i < min }
			}
			set_temp_variable = { min = BRA_develop_graph_values^i }
		}
	}
	set_temp_variable = { range = max }
	subtract_from_temp_variable = { range = min }

	# Determine rounding factor based on range
	set_temp_variable = { unit = 10000 }
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { range < 3 }
		}
		set_temp_variable = { unit = 1 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { range < 6 }
		}
		set_temp_variable = { unit = 2 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { range < 12 }
		}
		set_temp_variable = { unit = 5 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { range < 30 }
		}
		set_temp_variable = { unit = 15 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { range < 60 }
		}
		set_temp_variable = { unit = 40 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { range < 120 }
		}
		set_temp_variable = { unit = 80 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { range < 300 }
		}
		set_temp_variable = { unit = 150 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { range < 600 }
		}
		set_temp_variable = { unit = 400 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { range < 1200 }
		}
		set_temp_variable = { unit = 500 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { range < 3000 }
		}
		set_temp_variable = { unit = 1000 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { range < 6000 }
		}
		set_temp_variable = { unit = 4000 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { range < 12000 }
		}
		set_temp_variable = { unit = 8000 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { range < 30000 }
		}
		set_temp_variable = { unit = 10000 }
	}

	divide_temp_variable = { min = unit }
	divide_temp_variable = { max = unit }
	subtract_from_temp_variable = { min = 4 }
	add_to_temp_variable = { max = 4 }
	round_temp_variable = min
	round_temp_variable = max

	multiply_temp_variable = { min = unit }
	multiply_temp_variable = { max = unit }

	set_temp_variable = { range = max }
	subtract_from_temp_variable = { range = min }

	# Find the unit we should display next to the y axis ticks (ie K, M, B etc)
	set_variable = { BRA_develop_graph_display_unit = BRA_develop_graph_base_unit }
	set_temp_variable = { divisor = 1000 }
	while_loop_effect = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { divisor < min }
		}
		multiply_temp_variable = { divisor = 1000 }
		add_to_variable = { BRA_develop_graph_display_unit = 1 }
	}
	divide_temp_variable = { divisor = 1000 }

	# Generate the y axis ticks for our graph
	divide_temp_variable = { range = 100 }
	set_temp_variable = { m2 = max }
	add_to_temp_variable = { m2 = 0.25 }
	set_temp_variable = { k = min }
	while_loop_effect = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { k < m2 }
		}
		set_temp_variable = { label = k }
		divide_temp_variable = { label = divisor }
		add_to_array = { BRA_develop_graph_vbars = label }

		set_temp_variable = { offset = k }
		subtract_from_temp_variable = { offset = min }
		divide_temp_variable = { offset = range }
		multiply_temp_variable = { offset = -1.5 }
		add_to_array = { BRA_develop_graph_vbar_offsets = offset }

		add_to_temp_variable = { k = unit }
	}

	# Actually generate the graph line segments
	for_loop_effect = {
		start = 0
		end = 12
		value = i

		set_temp_variable = { j = i }
		add_to_temp_variable = { j = 1 }

		set_temp_variable = { vj = BRA_develop_graph_values^j }
		set_temp_variable = { vi = BRA_develop_graph_values^i }
		subtract_from_temp_variable = { vj = min }
		subtract_from_temp_variable = { vi = min }
		divide_temp_variable = { vj = range }
		divide_temp_variable = { vi = range }

		divide_temp_variable = { vj = 2 }
		divide_temp_variable = { vi = 2 }
		round_temp_variable = vi
		round_temp_variable = vj
		multiply_temp_variable = { vj = 2 }
		multiply_temp_variable = { vi = 2 }

		set_temp_variable = { delta = vj }
		subtract_from_temp_variable = { delta = vi }
		divide_temp_variable = { delta = 2 }
		round_temp_variable = delta
		add_to_temp_variable = { delta = 50 }

		set_temp_variable = { offset = vi }
		multiply_temp_variable = { offset = -1.5 }

		add_to_array = { BRA_develop_graph_offsets = offset }
		add_to_array = { BRA_develop_graph_deltas = delta }

		set_temp_variable = { ti = BRA_develop_graph_target_values^i }
		subtract_from_temp_variable = { ti = min }
		divide_temp_variable = { ti = range }

		divide_temp_variable = { ti = 2 }
		round_temp_variable = ti
		multiply_temp_variable = { ti = 2 }

		set_temp_variable = { target_offset = ti }
		multiply_temp_variable = { target_offset = -1.41 }

		add_to_array = { BRA_develop_graph_target_offsets = target_offset }
		add_to_array = { BRA_develop_graph_target_deltas = 50 }
	}
	set_temp_variable = { tes2 = BRA_develop_graph_offsets^num }
	subtract_from_temp_variable = { tes2 = 1 }
	set_variable = { BRA_map_graph_texticon_y = BRA_develop_graph_offsets^tes2 }
	add_to_variable = { BRA_map_graph_texticon_y = 135 }
	set_variable = { BRA_map_graph_target_texticon_y = BRA_develop_graph_target_offsets^tes2 }
	add_to_variable = { BRA_map_graph_target_texticon_y = 130 }

	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { BRA_develop_graph_deltas^tes2 < 50 }
		}
		set_temp_variable = { ermm = 50 }
		subtract_from_temp_variable = { ermm = BRA_develop_graph_deltas^tes2 }
		#add_to_temp_variable = { ermm = 40 }
		add_to_variable = { BRA_map_graph_texticon_y = ermm }
	}
	else_if ={
		limit = {
			check_variable = { BRA_map_graph_texticon_ys^tes2 = 50 }
		}
	}
	else = {
		set_temp_variable = { ermm = BRA_develop_graph_deltas^tes2 }
		subtract_from_temp_variable = { ermm = 50 }
		add_to_temp_variable = { ermm = 12 }
		subtract_from_variable = { BRA_map_graph_texticon_y = ermm }
	}
}

BRA_develop_select_region = {
	clear_array = BRA_is_region_selected
	clr_country_flag = BRA_viewing_megaproject
	resize_array = {
		array = BRA_is_region_selected
		value = 1
		size = 5
	}
	add_to_array = {
		array = BRA_is_region_selected
		index = BRA_develop_selected_region
		value = 2
	}

	clear_array = BRA_develop_selected_region_arr
	add_to_array = { BRA_develop_selected_region_arr = BRA_develop_selected_region }

	set_variable = { BRA_develop_frame = BRA_develop_selected_region }
	add_to_variable = { BRA_develop_frame = 1 }

	BRA_develop_ready_graph = yes
}

# Set up the initial region status
BRA_initialize_develop = {
	set_variable = { BRA_develop_selected_region = 1 }
	set_variable = { BRA_develop_regional_progress_amazonia = 5 }

	set_variable = { base_inflation_rate = 36.3 }

	BRA_develop_init_graph_data = yes
	BRA_initialize_illiteracy = yes
	BRA_develop_update_regional_progress = yes

	clr_country_flag = BRA_develop_highway_slowdown_1
	clr_country_flag = BRA_develop_highway_milestone_1
	clr_country_flag = BRA_develop_highway_slowdown_2
	clr_country_flag = BRA_develop_highway_milestone_2

	BRA_develop_select_region = yes

	set_temp_variable = { alert_id = token:Alert_BRA_Development }
	add_TNO_alert_unless_exists = yes

	set_variable = { AMAZONIA_REGION = 0 }
	set_variable = { NORTH_EAST_REGION = 1 }
	set_variable = { CENTRAL_WEST_REGION = 2 }
	set_variable = { SOUTH_EAST_REGION = 3 }
	set_variable = { SOUTH_REGION = 4 }
	set_variable = { GUIANA_REGION = 5 }

	set_variable = { TRANS_AMAZONIAN_HIGHWAY_MEGAPROJECT = 0 }
	set_variable = { BRASILIA_AIRPORT_MEGAPROJECT = 1 }
	set_variable = { RIO_SAO_PAULO_LINE_MEGAPROJECT = 2 }
	set_variable = { FERROVIA_NORTE_SUL_MEGAPROJECT = 3 }
	set_variable = { PERIMETRAL_NORTE_MEGAPROJECT = 4 }
	set_variable = { SISTEMA_AQUAVIARIO_AMAZONICO_MEGAPROJECT = 5 }
	set_variable = { MACAPA_CAYENNE_HIGHWAY_MEGAPROJECT = 6 }
	set_variable = { ITAIPU_HYDROELECTIC_DAM_MEGAPROJECT = 7 }
	set_variable = { SUS_HEALTHCARE_MEGAPROJECT = 8 }
	set_variable = { RIO_NITEROI_BRIDGE_MEGAPROJECT = 9 }
	set_variable = { ADHEMAR_LAND_REFORM_MEGAPROJECT = 10 }
	set_variable = { ADHEMAR_NUCLEAR_BASE_MEGAPROJECT = 11 }
	set_variable = { GUANABARA_RECONSTRUCTION_MEGAPROJECT = 12 }
	set_variable = { ANGRA_POWER_PLANT_MEGAPROJECT = 13 }

	clear_array = BRA_active_megaprojects
	add_to_array = { BRA_active_megaprojects = TRANS_AMAZONIAN_HIGHWAY_MEGAPROJECT }

	# Base Values
	clear_array = BRA_megaprojects_progress
	resize_array = { array = BRA_megaprojects_progress value = 0 size = 10 }
	clear_array = BRA_megaprojects_progress_next_month
	resize_array = { array = BRA_megaprojects_progress_next_month value = 0 size = BRA_megaprojects_progress^num }
	clear_array = BRA_megaprojects_level
	resize_array = { array = BRA_megaprojects_level value = 0 size = BRA_megaprojects_progress^num }
	clear_array = BRA_megaprojects_base_pp_cost
	resize_array = { array = BRA_megaprojects_base_pp_cost value = 0 size = BRA_megaprojects_progress^num }
	clear_array = BRA_megaprojects_pp_cost_per_level
	resize_array = { array = BRA_megaprojects_pp_cost_per_level value = 0 size = BRA_megaprojects_progress^num }
	clear_array = BRA_megaprojects_cost_per_level
	resize_array = { array = BRA_megaprojects_cost_per_level value = 0 size = BRA_megaprojects_progress^num }
	clear_array = BRA_megaprojects_max_level
	resize_array = { array = BRA_megaprojects_max_level value = 0 size = BRA_megaprojects_progress^num }
	clear_array = BRA_megaprojects_max_prog
	resize_array = { array = BRA_megaprojects_max_prog value = 0 size = BRA_megaprojects_progress^num }
	clear_array = BRA_megaprojects_region
	resize_array = { array = BRA_megaprojects_region value = 0 size = BRA_megaprojects_progress^num }
	clear_array = BRA_megaprojects_next_milestone
	resize_array = { array = BRA_megaprojects_next_milestone value = 0 size = BRA_megaprojects_progress^num }

	# Derived Values
	clear_array = BRA_megaprojects_cost
	resize_array = { array = BRA_megaprojects_cost value = 0 size = BRA_megaprojects_progress^num }
	clear_array = BRA_megaprojects_pp_cost
	resize_array = { array = BRA_megaprojects_pp_cost value = 0 size = BRA_megaprojects_progress^num }
	clear_array = BRA_megaprojects_pp_cost
	resize_array = { array = BRA_megaprojects_build_speed value = 0 size = BRA_megaprojects_progress^num }

	# Trans-Amazonian Highway
	set_variable = { BRA_megaprojects_level^TRANS_AMAZONIAN_HIGHWAY_MEGAPROJECT = 2 }
	set_variable = { BRA_megaprojects_max_level^TRANS_AMAZONIAN_HIGHWAY_MEGAPROJECT = 5 }
	set_variable = { BRA_megaprojects_pp_cost_per_level^TRANS_AMAZONIAN_HIGHWAY_MEGAPROJECT = 0.03 }
	set_variable = { BRA_megaprojects_cost_per_level^TRANS_AMAZONIAN_HIGHWAY_MEGAPROJECT = 0.060 }
	set_variable = { BRA_megaprojects_pu_cost_per_level^TRANS_AMAZONIAN_HIGHWAY_MEGAPROJECT = 2 }
	set_variable = { BRA_megaprojects_max_prog^TRANS_AMAZONIAN_HIGHWAY_MEGAPROJECT = 14.5 }
	set_variable = { BRA_megaprojects_region^TRANS_AMAZONIAN_HIGHWAY_MEGAPROJECT = AMAZONIA_REGION }
	set_variable = { BRA_megaprojects_progress^TRANS_AMAZONIAN_HIGHWAY_MEGAPROJECT = 18.1 } # Starts with some progress already


	# Airport
	set_variable = { BRA_megaprojects_level^BRASILIA_AIRPORT_MEGAPROJECT = 1 }
	set_variable = { BRA_megaprojects_max_level^BRASILIA_AIRPORT_MEGAPROJECT = 3 }
	set_variable = { BRA_megaprojects_pp_cost_per_level^BRASILIA_AIRPORT_MEGAPROJECT = 0.03 }
	set_variable = { BRA_megaprojects_cost_per_level^BRASILIA_AIRPORT_MEGAPROJECT = 0.050 }
	set_variable = { BRA_megaprojects_pu_cost_per_level^BRASILIA_AIRPORT_MEGAPROJECT = 2 }
	set_variable = { BRA_megaprojects_max_prog^BRASILIA_AIRPORT_MEGAPROJECT = 130 }
	set_variable = { BRA_megaprojects_region^BRASILIA_AIRPORT_MEGAPROJECT = CENTRAL_WEST_REGION }


	# Rio-Sao Paulo Line
	set_variable = { BRA_megaprojects_level^RIO_SAO_PAULO_LINE_MEGAPROJECT = 1 }
	set_variable = { BRA_megaprojects_max_level^RIO_SAO_PAULO_LINE_MEGAPROJECT = 5 }
	set_variable = { BRA_megaprojects_pp_cost_per_level^RIO_SAO_PAULO_LINE_MEGAPROJECT = 0.02 }
	set_variable = { BRA_megaprojects_cost_per_level^RIO_SAO_PAULO_LINE_MEGAPROJECT = 0.050 }
	set_variable = { BRA_megaprojects_pu_cost_per_level^RIO_SAO_PAULO_LINE_MEGAPROJECT = 2 }
	set_variable = { BRA_megaprojects_max_prog^RIO_SAO_PAULO_LINE_MEGAPROJECT = 18 }
	set_variable = { BRA_megaprojects_region^RIO_SAO_PAULO_LINE_MEGAPROJECT = SOUTH_EAST_REGION }

	# Ferrovia Norte-Sul
	set_variable = { BRA_megaprojects_level^FERROVIA_NORTE_SUL_MEGAPROJECT = 1 }
	set_variable = { BRA_megaprojects_max_level^FERROVIA_NORTE_SUL_MEGAPROJECT = 5 }
	set_variable = { BRA_megaprojects_pp_cost_per_level^FERROVIA_NORTE_SUL_MEGAPROJECT = 0.02 }
	set_variable = { BRA_megaprojects_cost_per_level^FERROVIA_NORTE_SUL_MEGAPROJECT = 0.015 }
	set_variable = { BRA_megaprojects_pu_cost_per_level^FERROVIA_NORTE_SUL_MEGAPROJECT = 2 }
	set_variable = { BRA_megaprojects_max_prog^FERROVIA_NORTE_SUL_MEGAPROJECT = 100 }
	set_variable = { BRA_megaprojects_region^FERROVIA_NORTE_SUL_MEGAPROJECT = NORTH_EAST_REGION }

	# Perimetral Norte
	set_variable = { BRA_megaprojects_level^PERIMETRAL_NORTE_MEGAPROJECT = 1 }
	set_variable = { BRA_megaprojects_max_level^PERIMETRAL_NORTE_MEGAPROJECT = 5 }
	set_variable = { BRA_megaprojects_base_pp_cost^PERIMETRAL_NORTE_MEGAPROJECT = 0.04 }
	set_variable = { BRA_megaprojects_pp_cost_per_level^PERIMETRAL_NORTE_MEGAPROJECT = 0.02 }
	set_variable = { BRA_megaprojects_cost_per_level^PERIMETRAL_NORTE_MEGAPROJECT = 0.015 }
	set_variable = { BRA_megaprojects_pu_cost_per_level^PERIMETRAL_NORTE_MEGAPROJECT = 2 }
	set_variable = { BRA_megaprojects_max_prog^PERIMETRAL_NORTE_MEGAPROJECT = 100 }
	set_variable = { BRA_megaprojects_region^PERIMETRAL_NORTE_MEGAPROJECT = AMAZONIA_REGION }

	# Sistema Aquaviário Amazônico
	set_variable = { BRA_megaprojects_level^SISTEMA_AQUAVIARIO_AMAZONICO_MEGAPROJECT = 1 }
	set_variable = { BRA_megaprojects_max_level^SISTEMA_AQUAVIARIO_AMAZONICO_MEGAPROJECT = 5 }
	set_variable = { BRA_megaprojects_pp_cost_per_level^SISTEMA_AQUAVIARIO_AMAZONICO_MEGAPROJECT = 0.02 }
	set_variable = { BRA_megaprojects_cost_per_level^SISTEMA_AQUAVIARIO_AMAZONICO_MEGAPROJECT = 0.015 }
	set_variable = { BRA_megaprojects_pu_cost_per_level^SISTEMA_AQUAVIARIO_AMAZONICO_MEGAPROJECT = 2 }
	set_variable = { BRA_megaprojects_max_prog^SISTEMA_AQUAVIARIO_AMAZONICO_MEGAPROJECT = 100 }
	set_variable = { BRA_megaprojects_region^SISTEMA_AQUAVIARIO_AMAZONICO_MEGAPROJECT = AMAZONIA_REGION }

	# Cayenne Highway
	set_variable = { BRA_megaprojects_level^MACAPA_CAYENNE_HIGHWAY_MEGAPROJECT = 1 }
	set_variable = { BRA_megaprojects_max_level^MACAPA_CAYENNE_HIGHWAY_MEGAPROJECT = 3 }

BRA_setup_selected_project_milestones = {
	set_temp_variable = { project_idx = BRA_develop_selected_project }
	BRA_setup_project_milestones = yes
}
BRA_selected_milestone_effect = {
	set_temp_variable = { project_idx = BRA_develop_selected_project }
	BRA_milestone_effect = yes
}

BRA_setup_project_milestones = {
	clear_array = BRA_megaprojects_milestones

	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { BRA_develop_selected_project = TRANS_AMAZONIAN_HIGHWAY_MEGAPROJECT } }
		BRA_setup_amazon_highway_milestones = yes
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { BRA_develop_selected_project = BRASILIA_AIRPORT_MEGAPROJECT } }
		BRA_setup_brasilia_airport_milestones = yes
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { BRA_develop_selected_project = MACAPA_CAYENNE_HIGHWAY_MEGAPROJECT } }
		BRA_setup_cayenne_highway_milestones = yes
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { BRA_develop_selected_project = ITAIPU_HYDROELECTIC_DAM_MEGAPROJECT } }
		BRA_setup_itaipu_hydrodam_milestones = yes
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { BRA_develop_selected_project = RIO_SAO_PAULO_LINE_MEGAPROJECT } }
		BRA_setup_rio_sao_highspeedrail_milestones = yes
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { BRA_develop_selected_project = RIO_NITEROI_BRIDGE_MEGAPROJECT } }
		BRA_setup_rio_niteroi_bridge_milestones = yes
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { BRA_develop_selected_project = SUS_HEALTHCARE_MEGAPROJECT } }
		BRA_setup_sus_healthcare_milestones = yes
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { BRA_develop_selected_project = ADHEMAR_LAND_REFORM_MEGAPROJECT } }
		BRA_setup_adhemar_land_reform_milestones = yes
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { BRA_develop_selected_project = ADHEMAR_NUCLEAR_BASE_MEGAPROJECT } }
		BRA_setup_nuclear_base_milestones = yes
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { BRA_develop_selected_project = GUANABARA_RECONSTRUCTION_MEGAPROJECT } }
		BRA_setup_guanabara_reconstruction_milestones = yes
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { BRA_develop_selected_project = ANGRA_POWER_PLANT_MEGAPROJECT } }
		BRA_setup_angra_plant_milestones = yes
	}

	clear_array = BRA_megaprojects_milestone_positions
	for_each_loop = {
		array = BRA_megaprojects_milestones
		value = amount

		set_temp_variable = { position = amount }
		multiply_temp_variable = { position = 2.75 }
		add_to_array = { BRA_megaprojects_milestone_positions = position }
	}
}


BRA_milestone_effect = {
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { BRA_develop_selected_project = TRANS_AMAZONIAN_HIGHWAY_MEGAPROJECT } }
		BRA_amazon_highway_milestone_effect = yes
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { BRA_develop_selected_project = BRASILIA_AIRPORT_MEGAPROJECT } }
		BRA_brasilia_airport_milestone_effect = yes
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { BRA_develop_selected_project = MACAPA_CAYENNE_HIGHWAY_MEGAPROJECT } }
		BRA_cayenne_highway_milestone_effect = yes
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { BRA_develop_selected_project = ITAIPU_HYDROELECTIC_DAM_MEGAPROJECT } }
		BRA_itaipu_hydrodam_milestone_effect = yes
	}
	else_if = {

		BRA_rio_sao_highspeedrail_milestone_effect = yes
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { BRA_develop_selected_project = RIO_NITEROI_BRIDGE_MEGAPROJECT } }
		BRA_rio_niteroi_bridge_milestone_effect = yes
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { BRA_develop_selected_project = SUS_HEALTHCARE_MEGAPROJECT } }
		BRA_sus_healthcare_milestone_effect = yes
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { BRA_develop_selected_project = ADHEMAR_LAND_REFORM_MEGAPROJECT } }
		BRA_adhemar_land_reform_milestone_effect = yes
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { BRA_develop_selected_project = ADHEMAR_NUCLEAR_BASE_MEGAPROJECT } }

	}
}


BRA_setup_cayenne_highway_milestones = {
	add_to_array = { BRA_megaprojects_milestones = 25 }
	add_to_array = { BRA_megaprojects_milestones = 55 }
	add_to_array = { BRA_megaprojects_milestones = 75 }
	add_to_array = { BRA_megaprojects_milestones = 100 }
}
BRA_cayenne_highway_milestone_effect = {
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { milestone_idx = 0 } }
		1482 = {
			add_building_construction = {
				type = infrastructure
				level = 1
				instant_build = yes
			}
			set_temp_variable = { state_value_multiplier_temp = 1.025 }
			econ_state_value_change_multiply = yes
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { milestone_idx = 1 } }
		1482 = {
			add_building_construction = {
				type = infrastructure
				level = 1
				instant_build = yes
			}
			set_temp_variable = { state_value_multiplier_temp = 1.02 }
			econ_state_value_change_multiply_specified_state = yes
		}
		BRA_develop_increase_industry_amazonia_low = yes
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { milestone_idx = 2 } }
		310 = {
			add_building_construction = {
				type = infrastructure
				level = 1
				instant_build = yes
			}
			set_temp_variable = { state_value_multiplier_temp = 1.025 }
			econ_state_value_change_multiply = yes
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { milestone_idx = 3 } }
		country_event = brazil.583
		310 = {
			add_building_construction = {
				type = infrastructure
				level = 1
				instant_build = yes
			}
			set_temp_variable = { state_value_multiplier_temp = 1.04 }
			econ_state_value_change_multiply_specified_state = yes
		}
	}
}

				level = 1

			}

		}

	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { milestone_idx = 1 } }
		503 = {
			add_manpower = -5000
			set_temp_variable = { state_value_multiplier_temp = 0.98 }
			econ_state_value_change_multiply_specified_state = yes
		}
		1531 = {
			add_manpower = 5000
		}
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = brazil.530 } }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { milestone_idx = 2 } }
		country_event = { id = brazil.531 }
		BRA_develop_increase_industry_south_low = yes
		503 = {
			add_building_construction = {
				type = barracks
				level = 1
				instant_build = yes
			}
		}
		1531 = {
			set_temp_variable = { state_value_multiplier_temp = 1.05 }
			econ_state_value_change_multiply = yes
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { milestone_idx = 3 } }
		add_resource = {
			type = power
			amount = 6
			state = 503
		}
		TNO_improve_industrial_expertise_low = yes
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = brazil.532 } }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { milestone_idx = 4 } }
		503 = {
			add_building_construction = {
				type = infrastructure
				level = 1
				instant_build = yes
			}
			set_temp_variable = { state_value_multiplier_temp = 1.06 }
			econ_state_value_change_multiply_specified_state = yes
			add_building_construction = {
				type = hydroelectric_plant
				level = 1
				instant_build = yes
			}
		}
		1620 = {
			add_building_construction = {
				type = infrastructure
				level = 1
				instant_build = yes
			}
			set_temp_variable = { state_value_multiplier_temp = 1.06 }
			econ_state_value_change_multiply_specified_state = yes
		}
		PAR = {
			set_temp_variable = { gdp_growth_temp = 1.2 }
			econ_gdp_growth_change = yes
		}
		hidden_effect = {

				amount = -7

			}

			amount = 8
			state = 1620
		}

	}

BRA_rio_niteroi_bridge_milestone_effect = {
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { milestone_idx = 0 } }
		country_event = { id = brazil.550 }
		TNO_improve_industrial_equipment_low = yes
		TNO_improve_industrial_expertise_low = yes
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { milestone_idx = 1 } }
		1488 = {
			set_temp_variable = { state_value_multiplier_temp = 1.01 }
			econ_state_value_change_multiply_specified_state = yes
			add_state_modifier = { modifier = { state_GDP_growth_modifier = 0.35 } }
			}
		}
	else_if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { milestone_idx = 2 } }
		country_event = { id = brazil.551 }
		BRA_develop_increase_industry_monthly_southeast_low = yes
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { milestone_idx = 3 } }
		1488 = {
			add_building_construction = {

BRA_develop_update_projects = {
	set_variable = { BRA_megaproject_pus = 0 }
	set_variable = { BRA_develop_pp_cost = 0 }
	set_variable = { BRA_megaproject_cost = 0 }
	for_each_loop = {
		array = BRA_active_megaprojects
		value = project_idx

		set_variable = { BRA_megaprojects_cost^project_idx = BRA_megaprojects_level^project_idx }
		multiply_variable = { BRA_megaprojects_cost^project_idx = BRA_megaprojects_cost_per_level^project_idx }

		set_variable = { BRA_megaprojects_pp_cost^project_idx = BRA_megaprojects_level^project_idx }
		multiply_variable = { BRA_megaprojects_pp_cost^project_idx = BRA_megaprojects_pp_cost_per_level^project_idx }

		set_variable = { BRA_megaprojects_pus^project_idx = BRA_megaprojects_level^project_idx }
		multiply_variable = { BRA_megaprojects_pus^project_idx = BRA_megaprojects_pu_cost_per_level^project_idx }

		subtract_from_variable = { BRA_megaproject_pus = BRA_megaprojects_pus^project_idx }

		add_to_variable = { BRA_megaproject_cost = BRA_megaprojects_cost^project_idx }
		add_to_variable = { BRA_develop_pp_cost = BRA_megaprojects_pp_cost^project_idx }

		set_temp_variable = { build_speed = BRA_megaprojects_max_prog^project_idx }
		multiply_temp_variable = { build_speed = BRA_megaprojects_level^project_idx }
		divide_temp_variable = { build_speed = BRA_megaprojects_max_level^project_idx }

		set_temp_variable = { build_speed_multiplier = modifier@BRA_megaproject_construction_speed }
		add_to_temp_variable = { build_speed_multiplier = 1 }
		multiply_temp_variable = { build_speed = build_speed_multiplier }

		set_variable = { BRA_megaprojects_build_speed^project_idx = build_speed }

		set_variable = { BRA_megaprojects_progress_next_month^project_idx = BRA_megaprojects_progress^project_idx }
		set_temp_variable = { monthly = BRA_megaprojects_build_speed^project_idx }
		divide_temp_variable = { monthly = 12 }
		add_to_variable = { BRA_megaprojects_progress_next_month^project_idx = monthly }

		clamp_variable = { var = BRA_megaprojects_progress^project_idx min = 0 max = 100 }
		clamp_variable = { var = BRA_megaprojects_progress_next_month^project_idx min = 0 max = 100 }

		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { BRA_megaprojects_progress^project_idx = BRA_megaprojects_max_prog^project_idx }
			}
			set_variable = {
				BRA_megaprojects_level^project_idx = 0
			}
		}
	}

	# Cayenne Highway
	set_variable = { BRA_develop_cayenne_highway_frame = BRA_megaprojects_progress^MACAPA_CAYENNE_HIGHWAY_MEGAPROJECT }
	divide_variable = { BRA_develop_cayenne_highway_frame = 10 }


	# Highway-specific stuff
	set_variable = { BRA_develop_highway_cost = BRA_megaprojects_cost^TRANS_AMAZONIAN_HIGHWAY_MEGAPROJECT }



	set_variable = { BRA_develop_highway_pus = BRA_megaprojects_level^TRANS_AMAZONIAN_HIGHWAY_MEGAPROJECT }
	set_variable = { BRA_develop_highway_pus_display = BRA_develop_highway_pus }
	multiply_variable = { BRA_develop_highway_pus = -1 }

	# set_variable = { BRA_develop_highway_level_prev = BRA_develop_highway_level }

	set_variable = { BRA_develop_highway_frame = 100 }
	subtract_from_variable = { BRA_develop_highway_frame = BRA_megaprojects_progress^TRANS_AMAZONIAN_HIGHWAY_MEGAPROJECT }
	divide_variable = { BRA_develop_highway_frame = 100 }
	multiply_variable = { BRA_develop_highway_frame = 9.5 }

	add_to_variable = { BRA_develop_highway_frame = 1.4 }
	round_variable = BRA_develop_highway_frame
}

# please tell me we're reworking the megaproject backend post c&b
BRA_setup_project_milestones_monthly = {
	clear_array = BRA_megaprojects_milestones
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { project_idx = TRANS_AMAZONIAN_HIGHWAY_MEGAPROJECT } }
		BRA_setup_amazon_highway_milestones = yes
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { project_idx = BRASILIA_AIRPORT_MEGAPROJECT } }
		BRA_setup_brasilia_airport_milestones = yes
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { project_idx = MACAPA_CAYENNE_HIGHWAY_MEGAPROJECT } }
		BRA_setup_cayenne_highway_milestones = yes
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { project_idx = ITAIPU_HYDROELECTIC_DAM_MEGAPROJECT } }
		BRA_setup_itaipu_hydrodam_milestones = yes
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { project_idx = RIO_SAO_PAULO_LINE_MEGAPROJECT } }
		BRA_setup_rio_sao_highspeedrail_milestones = yes
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { project_idx = RIO_NITEROI_BRIDGE_MEGAPROJECT } }
		BRA_setup_rio_niteroi_bridge_milestones = yes
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { project_idx = SUS_HEALTHCARE_MEGAPROJECT } }
		BRA_setup_sus_healthcare_milestones = yes
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { project_idx = ADHEMAR_LAND_REFORM_MEGAPROJECT } }
		BRA_setup_adhemar_land_reform_milestones = yes
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { project_idx = ADHEMAR_NUCLEAR_BASE_MEGAPROJECT } }
		BRA_setup_nuclear_base_milestones = yes
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { project_idx = GUANABARA_RECONSTRUCTION_MEGAPROJECT } }
		BRA_setup_guanabara_reconstruction_milestones = yes
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { project_idx = ANGRA_POWER_PLANT_MEGAPROJECT } }
		BRA_setup_angra_plant_milestones = yes
	}
}

BRA_milestone_effect_monthly = {
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { project_idx = TRANS_AMAZONIAN_HIGHWAY_MEGAPROJECT } }
		BRA_amazon_highway_milestone_effect = yes
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { project_idx = BRASILIA_AIRPORT_MEGAPROJECT } }
		BRA_brasilia_airport_milestone_effect = yes
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { project_idx = MACAPA_CAYENNE_HIGHWAY_MEGAPROJECT } }
		BRA_cayenne_highway_milestone_effect = yes
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { project_idx = ITAIPU_HYDROELECTIC_DAM_MEGAPROJECT } }
		BRA_itaipu_hydrodam_milestone_effect = yes
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { project_idx = RIO_SAO_PAULO_LINE_MEGAPROJECT } }
		BRA_rio_sao_highspeedrail_milestone_effect = yes
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { project_idx = RIO_NITEROI_BRIDGE_MEGAPROJECT } }
		BRA_rio_niteroi_bridge_milestone_effect = yes
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { project_idx = SUS_HEALTHCARE_MEGAPROJECT } }
		BRA_sus_healthcare_milestone_effect = yes
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { project_idx = ADHEMAR_LAND_REFORM_MEGAPROJECT } }
		BRA_adhemar_land_reform_milestone_effect = yes
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { project_idx = ADHEMAR_NUCLEAR_BASE_MEGAPROJECT } }
		BRA_nuclear_base_milestone_effect = yes
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { project_idx = GUANABARA_RECONSTRUCTION_MEGAPROJECT } }
		BRA_guanabara_reconstruction_milestone_effect = yes
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { project_idx = ANGRA_POWER_PLANT_MEGAPROJECT } }
		BRA_angra_plant_milestone_effect = yes
	}
}

BRA_develop_project_monthly = {
	for_each_loop = {
		array = BRA_active_megaprojects
		value = project_idx

		set_temp_variable = { monthly = BRA_megaprojects_build_speed^project_idx }
		divide_temp_variable = { monthly = 12 }
		set_temp_variable = { temp_add = 1 }
		add_to_temp_variable = { temp_add = BRA_lacerda_samba_project_boost }
		multiply_temp_variable = { monthly = temp_add }

		add_to_variable = { BRA_megaprojects_progress^project_idx = monthly }
		clamp_variable = { var = BRA_megaprojects_progress^project_idx min = 0 max = 100 }

		set_temp_variable = { monthly = BRA_megaprojects_cost^project_idx }
		divide_temp_variable = { monthly = 12 }

		set_temp_variable = { temp_econ_spending_amount = monthly }
		econ_spend_money_once_effect_raw_money = yes

		# milestones stuff
		BRA_setup_project_milestones_monthly = yes
		while_loop_effect = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { BRA_megaprojects_next_milestone^project_idx < BRA_megaprojects_milestones^num }
				check_variable = { var = BRA_megaprojects_progress^project_idx value = BRA_megaprojects_milestones^BRA_megaprojects_next_milestone^project_idx compare = greater_than_or_equals }
			}
			set_temp_variable = { milestone_idx = BRA_megaprojects_next_milestone^project_idx }
			add_to_variable = { BRA_megaprojects_next_milestone^project_idx = 1 }
			BRA_milestone_effect_monthly = yes
		}
	}

	BRA_develop_update_projects = yes

	# Highway stuff
	set_temp_variable = { highway_progress = BRA_megaprojects_progress^TRANS_AMAZONIAN_HIGHWAY_MEGAPROJECT }
}


BRA_update_active_project_display = {
	clear_array = BRA_active_display

	for_loop_effect = {
		start = 0
		end = BRA_active_megaprojects^num
		value = i

		add_to_array = { BRA_active_display = BRA_active_megaprojects^i }
	}

	set_temp_variable = { num_active = BRA_active_display^num }
	modulo_temp_variable = { num_active = 10 }

	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { num_active = 1 } }

		set_temp_variable = { insert_idx = BRA_active_display^num }
		# subtract_from_variable = { insert_idx = 2 }
		add_to_array = { array = BRA_active_display value = -1 index = 0 }
	}
}


BRA_develop_increase_highway_pp = {
	custom_effect_tooltip = BRA_increase_highway_pp_tt

	add_to_variable = { BRA_megaprojects_base_pp_cost^TRANS_AMAZONIAN_HIGHWAY_MEGAPROJECT = 0.05 }

	BRA_develop_update_projects = yes
}


BRA_develop_update_regional_progress = {
	clear_array = BRA_develop_regional_progress
	add_to_array = { BRA_develop_regional_progress = BRA_develop_regional_progress_amazonia }

	set_temp_variable = { curr = 0 }
	set_temp_variable = { divisor = 0 }

	set_variable = { BRA_development_monthly_population = 0 }
	set_variable = { BRA_development_taxable_population_modifier = 0}

	for_loop_effect = {
		start = 1
		end = 5
		value = i

		clamp_variable = { var = BRA_develop_region_urban_pop^i min = 0 max = 100 }
		clamp_variable = { var = BRA_develop_region_industry^i min = 0 max = 100 }
		clamp_variable = { var = BRA_develop_region_mech_rate^i min = 0 max = 100 }

		add_to_variable = { BRA_development_monthly_population = BRA_develop_region_mech_rate^i }
		add_to_variable = { BRA_development_taxable_population_modifier = BRA_develop_region_industry^i }

		set_temp_variable = { pop_pct = BRA_develop_region_urban_pop^i }
		set_temp_variable = { industry_pct = BRA_develop_region_industry^i }
		set_temp_variable = { mech_rate = BRA_develop_region_mech_rate^i }
		clamp_temp_variable = { var = pop_pct min = 0 max = 70 }
		clamp_temp_variable = { var = industry_pct min = 0 max = 50 }
		clamp_temp_variable = { var = mech_rate min = 0 max = 60 }
		divide_temp_variable = { pop_pct = 210 }
		divide_temp_variable = { industry_pct = 150 }
		divide_temp_variable = { mech_rate = 180 }

		set_temp_variable = { progress_total = pop_pct }
		add_to_temp_variable = { progress_total = industry_pct }
		add_to_temp_variable = { progress_total = mech_rate }
		multiply_temp_variable = { progress_total = 6 }
		add_to_temp_variable = { progress_total = -1 }
		round_temp_variable = progress_total
		add_to_array = { BRA_develop_regional_progress = progress_total }


		set_temp_variable = { to_add = BRA_develop_region_industry^i }
		divide_temp_variable = { to_add = 100 }
		multiply_temp_variable = { to_add = BRA_develop_region_pop_history^12 }
		add_to_temp_variable = { current = to_add }

		set_temp_variable = { pop_to_add = BRA_develop_region_pop_history^12 }
		divide_temp_variable = { pop_to_add = 100 }
		add_to_temp_variable = { divisor = pop_to_add }
	}
	divide_variable = { BRA_development_monthly_population = 2000 }
	divide_variable = { BRA_development_taxable_population_modifier = 5000 }
	force_update_dynamic_modifier = yes
	divide_temp_variable = { current = divisor }
	set_variable = { BRA_develop_industry_pct_gdp = current }
}

							state_GDP_growth_factor_modifier = 0.03
						}
					}
					add_to_variable = { Mech_State_Boost = 1 }
				}
			}
			10 = {
				modifier = {
					factor = 0
					280 = { check_variable = { Mech_State_Boost > 4 } }
				}
				280 = {

					}

###############################################################
########           Presidential Race Mechanic          ########

BRA_pres_select_region = {
	clear_array = BRA_is_region_selected_pres
	resize_array = {
		array = BRA_is_region_selected_pres
		value = 1
		size = 9
	}
	add_to_array = {
		array = BRA_is_region_selected_pres
		index = BRA_pres_selected_region
		value = 2
	}

	clear_array = BRA_pres_selected_pops
	clear_array = BRA_pres_selected_momentum

	set_temp_variable = { lo = BRA_pres_selected_region }
	multiply_temp_variable = { lo = BRA_pres_candidates^num }
	set_temp_variable = { hi = lo }
	add_to_temp_variable = { hi = BRA_pres_candidates^num }
	for_loop_effect = {
		start = lo
		end = hi
		value = i

		set_temp_variable = { support = BRA_pres_support^i }
		divide_temp_variable = { support = 10 }
		add_to_array = { BRA_pres_selected_pops = support }
		add_to_array = { BRA_pres_selected_momentum = BRA_pres_momentum^i }
	}

	set_temp_variable = { my_pres_idx = BRA_pres_selected_region }
	multiply_temp_variable = { my_pres_idx = BRA_pres_candidates^num }

	for_loop_effect = {
		start = 0
		end = BRA_pres_candidates^num
		value = i

		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { BRA_pres_candidates^i = BRA_pres_chosen_candidate } }
			add_to_temp_variable = { my_pres_idx = i }
			set_variable = { BRA_pres_chosen_candidate_index = i }
			set_variable = { BRA_pres_chosen_candidate_party_display = BRA_pres_candidate_parties^i }
		}
	}
	set_variable = { BRA_pres_current_state_infra = BRA_pres_infra^my_pres_idx }
	set_variable = { BRA_pres_current_state_fatigue = BRA_pres_fatigue^BRA_pres_selected_region }
	set_variable = { BRA_pres_current_state_fatigue_display = 1 }
	subtract_from_variable = { BRA_pres_current_state_fatigue_display = BRA_pres_current_state_fatigue }

	#BRA_develop_ready_graph = yes
}

BRA_initialize_pres = {
	clear_array = BRA_numbers_to_hundred

	for_loop_effect = {
		start = 0
		end = 101
		add = 20
		value = i

		add_to_array = { BRA_numbers_to_hundred = i }
	}


	clear_array = BRA_pres_candidates
	clear_array = BRA_pres_candidate_parties
	clear_array = BRA_pres_support
	clear_array = BRA_pres_momentum
	clear_array = BRA_pres_infra

	BRA_initialize_pres_region_pop = yes
	BRA_redraw_pres_info = yes
	BRA_pres_select_region = yes

	# BRA_pres_start_65_election = yes

	clear_array = BRA_pres_campaigning_party
	resize_array = { array = BRA_pres_campaigning_party size = 9 value = 0 }
	clear_array = BRA_pres_campaigning_party_2
	resize_array = { array = BRA_pres_campaigning_party_2 size = 9 value = 0 }
}

BRA_pres_weekly_tick = {
	for_loop_effect = {
		start = 0
		end = 9
		value = i

		set_temp_variable = { lo = i }
		multiply_temp_variable = { lo = BRA_pres_candidates^num }

		for_loop_effect = {
			start = 0
			end = BRA_pres_candidates^num
			value = j

			set_temp_variable = { support_idx = j }
			add_to_temp_variable = { support_idx = lo }

			set_temp_variable = { delta = BRA_pres_momentum^support_idx }
			multiply_temp_variable = { delta = 300 }
			divide_temp_variable = { delta = BRA_pres_region_pop^i }
			multiply_temp_variable = { delta = 100 }

			add_to_variable = { BRA_pres_support^support_idx = delta }
			multiply_variable = { BRA_pres_momentum^support_idx = 0.8 }

		}
	}
	for_loop_effect = {
		start = 0
		end = 9
		value = i

		add_to_variable = { BRA_pres_fatigue^i = 0.1 }
		clamp_variable = { var = BRA_pres_fatigue^i min = 0 max = 1 }
	}
	BRA_redraw_pres_info = yes
	BRA_pres_select_region = yes
}

BRA_pres_others_campaign = {

	log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Beginning campaign process"

	clear_temp_array = BRA_taken_regions

	for_loop_effect = {
		start = 0
		end = BRA_pres_candidates^num
		value = k

		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { check_variable = { BRA_pres_chosen_candidate = BRA_pres_candidates^k } }
			}

			set_temp_variable = { chosen_region = 9 }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { chosen_region = BRA_taken_regions^num }
			multiply_temp_variable = { chosen_region = random }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { chosen_region = 0.5 }
			round_temp_variable = chosen_region

			while_loop_effect = {
				limit = { is_in_array = { BRA_taken_regions = chosen_region } }
				add_to_temp_variable = { chosen_region = 1 }
			}


			set_temp_variable = { what_do = random }
			round_temp_variable = what_do

			# AI decides to rally (up popularity directly)
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { what_do = 0 } }

				set_temp_variable = { idx = chosen_region }
				multiply_temp_variable = { idx = BRA_pres_candidates^num }
				add_to_temp_variable = { idx = k }

				# Rallies are more effective in lower pop. states
				set_temp_variable = { amount = 540000 }
				divide_temp_variable = { amount = BRA_pres_region_pop^chosen_region }
				# Fatigue reduces effectiveness
				multiply_temp_variable = { amount = BRA_pres_fatigue^chosen_region }

				add_to_variable = { BRA_pres_support^idx = amount }
			}
			# AI decides to campaign (up momentum)
			else = {
				set_temp_variable = { idx = chosen_region }
				multiply_temp_variable = { idx = BRA_pres_candidates^num }
				add_to_temp_variable = { idx = k }

				# Campaigning is the same strength in each state, but the momentum tick
				# will be weaker for more populous states
				set_temp_variable = { amount = 13.5 }
				# Fatigue reduces effectiveness
				multiply_temp_variable = { amount = BRA_pres_fatigue^chosen_region }
				add_to_variable = { BRA_pres_momentum^idx = amount }
			}

			subtract_from_variable = { BRA_pres_fatigue^chosen_region = 0.1 }
			clamp_variable = { var = BRA_pres_fatigue^chosen_region min = 0 max = 1 }

			set_variable = { BRA_pres_campaigning_party^chosen_region = BRA_pres_candidate_parties^k }

			add_to_temp_array = { BRA_taken_regions = chosen_region }
		}
	}
	BRA_redraw_pres_info = yes
	BRA_pres_select_region = yes

	hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = brazil.251 days = 14 } }
}

	add_to_temp_variable = { population = 1491.state_population_k }
	add_to_temp_variable = { population = 1492.state_population_k }
	add_to_array = { BRA_pres_region_total_pop = population }
	set_temp_variable = { BRA_pres_region_total_pop_show = population }
	divide_temp_variable = { BRA_pres_region_total_pop_show = 1000 }
	add_to_array = { BRA_pres_region_total_pop_show = BRA_pres_region_total_pop_show }
	set_temp_variable = { x = BRA_illiteracy_array^6 }
	subtract_from_temp_variable = { x = 100 }
	multiply_temp_variable = { x = -1 }
	multiply_temp_variable = { population = x }
	divide_temp_variable = { population = 100 }
	round_temp_variable = population
	add_to_array = { BRA_pres_region_pop = population }
	set_temp_variable = { region_pop_show = population }
	divide_temp_variable = { region_pop_show = 1000 }
	add_to_array = { BRA_pres_region_pop_show = region_pop_show }
	set_temp_variable_to_random = {
		var = BRA_voting_turnout_temp
		max = 90
		min = 50
	}
	add_to_array = { BRA_pres_region_voting_turnout = BRA_voting_turnout_temp }
	set_temp_variable = { BRA_voting_pop = population }
	divide_temp_variable = { BRA_voting_turnout_temp = 100 }
	multiply_temp_variable = { BRA_voting_pop = BRA_voting_turnout_temp }
	add_to_array = { BRA_pres_region_voting_pop = BRA_voting_pop }
	set_temp_variable = { BRA_voting_pop_show = BRA_voting_pop }
	divide_temp_variable = { BRA_voting_pop_show = 1000 }
	add_to_array = { BRA_pres_region_voting_pop_show = BRA_voting_pop_show }

	#RJ-ES
	set_temp_variable = { population = 500.state_population_k }
	add_to_temp_variable = { population = 1487.state_population_k }
	add_to_temp_variable = { population = 1488.state_population_k }
	add_to_array = { BRA_pres_region_total_pop = population }
	set_temp_variable = { BRA_pres_region_total_pop_show = population }
	divide_temp_variable = { BRA_pres_region_total_pop_show = 1000 }
	add_to_array = { BRA_pres_region_total_pop_show = BRA_pres_region_total_pop_show }
	set_temp_variable = { x = BRA_illiteracy_array^7 }
	subtract_from_temp_variable = { x = 100 }
	multiply_temp_variable = { x = -1 }
	multiply_temp_variable = { population = x }
	divide_temp_variable = { population = 100 }
	round_temp_variable = population
	add_to_array = { BRA_pres_region_pop = population }
	set_temp_variable = { region_pop_show = population }
	divide_temp_variable = { region_pop_show = 1000 }
	add_to_array = { BRA_pres_region_pop_show = region_pop_show }
	set_temp_variable_to_random = {
		var = BRA_voting_turnout_temp
		max = 90
		min = 50
	}
	add_to_array = { BRA_pres_region_voting_turnout = BRA_voting_turnout_temp }
	set_temp_variable = { BRA_voting_pop = population }
	divide_temp_variable = { BRA_voting_turnout_temp = 100 }
	multiply_temp_variable = { BRA_voting_pop = BRA_voting_turnout_temp }
	add_to_array = { BRA_pres_region_voting_pop = BRA_voting_pop }
	set_temp_variable = { BRA_voting_pop_show = BRA_voting_pop }
	divide_temp_variable = { BRA_voting_pop_show = 1000 }
	add_to_array = { BRA_pres_region_voting_pop_show = BRA_voting_pop_show }

	#Sao Paulo
	set_temp_variable = { population = 501.state_population_k }
	add_to_array = { BRA_pres_region_total_pop = population }
	set_temp_variable = { BRA_pres_region_total_pop_show = population }
	divide_temp_variable = { BRA_pres_region_total_pop_show = 1000 }
	add_to_array = { BRA_pres_region_total_pop_show = BRA_pres_region_total_pop_show }
	set_temp_variable = { x = BRA_illiteracy_array^8 }
	subtract_from_temp_variable = { x = 100 }
	multiply_temp_variable = { x = -1 }
	multiply_temp_variable = { population = x }
	divide_temp_variable = { population = 100 }
	round_temp_variable = population
	add_to_array = { BRA_pres_region_pop = population }
	set_temp_variable = { region_pop_show = population }
	divide_temp_variable = { region_pop_show = 1000 }
	add_to_array = { BRA_pres_region_pop_show = region_pop_show }
	set_temp_variable_to_random = {
		var = BRA_voting_turnout_temp
		max = 90
		min = 50
	}
	add_to_array = { BRA_pres_region_voting_turnout = BRA_voting_turnout_temp }
	set_temp_variable = { BRA_voting_pop = population }
	divide_temp_variable = { BRA_voting_turnout_temp = 100 }
	multiply_temp_variable = { BRA_voting_pop = BRA_voting_turnout_temp }
	add_to_array = { BRA_pres_region_voting_pop = BRA_voting_pop }
	set_temp_variable = { BRA_voting_pop_show = BRA_voting_pop }
	divide_temp_variable = { BRA_voting_pop_show = 1000 }
	add_to_array = { BRA_pres_region_voting_pop_show = BRA_voting_pop_show }
}

BRA_pres_start_65_election = {

	###################
	# RESETTING STUFF #
	###################

	# Resets all various arrays
	clear_array = BRA_pres_candidates
	clear_array = BRA_pres_candidate_parties
	clear_array = BRA_pres_support
	clear_array = BRA_pres_infra
	clear_array = BRA_pres_fatigue
	clear_array = BRA_pres_momentum

	# Ensures we get the right popular vote tallies for each state
	# in case population has changed since last election
	BRA_initialize_pres_region_pop = yes

	# Prepare support array
	# Size 27 because of 9 regions and 3 candidates
	resize_array = { array = BRA_pres_support size = 27 value = 0 }

	####################
	# SETUP CANDIDATES #
	####################

	# Here we decide who the PSD/PTB candidate is
	# in this case it's Goulart if the BRA_65_goulart_candidate flag is set

	if = { # goulart
		limit = { has_country_flag = BRA_65_goulart_candidate }

		# Add Goulart as the first candidate, he has id '0'
		# this id matches the scripted localization entries for
		# BRA_pres_candidate_name and BRA_pres_candidate_portrait
		# which in turn selects the loc BRA_pres_candidate_name_0

		add_to_array = { BRA_pres_candidates = 0 }

		# This sets up Goulart to run with the PTB
		add_to_array = { BRA_pres_candidate_parties = PARTY_PTB }

		# Set up Goulart's support in the various regions
		# the raw numbers don't matter, this is just relative to the other candidates
		# Since Goulart is the first candidate, we start with 0, and then add 3 for each region
		# since there are 3 other candidates in the 1965 elections

		set_variable = { BRA_pres_support^0 = 50 } # Amazonia
		set_variable = { BRA_pres_support^3 = 42 } # Bahia
		set_variable = { BRA_pres_support^6 = 30 } # Central-West
		set_variable = { BRA_pres_support^9 = 36 } # Minas Gerais
		set_variable = { BRA_pres_support^12 = 50 } # South
		set_variable = { BRA_pres_support^15 = 37 } # Maranhao-Piaui
		set_variable = { BRA_pres_support^18 = 35 } # Northeast
		set_variable = { BRA_pres_support^21 = 29 } # RJ-ES

		# Here we adjust Goulart's support based on the various events

		# Is Quadros running? if so Goulart loses support in Sao Paulo
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = BRA_65_quadros_candidate
			}
			set_variable = { BRA_pres_support^24 = 27 } # Sao Paulo
		}
		else = {
			set_variable = { BRA_pres_support^24 = 30 }
		}

		# If Goulart had won the Hundred Days' he gains support
		if = { # Jango becomes more popular
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = BRA_goulart_wins_hundred_days
			}
			add_to_variable = { BRA_pres_support^0 = 2 }
			add_to_variable = { BRA_pres_support^3 = 1 }
			add_to_variable = { BRA_pres_support^6 = 1 }
			add_to_variable = { BRA_pres_support^9 = 4 }
			add_to_variable = { BRA_pres_support^12 = 5 }
			add_to_variable = { BRA_pres_support^15 = 3 }
			add_to_variable = { BRA_pres_support^18 = 1 }
			add_to_variable = { BRA_pres_support^21 = 1 }
			add_to_variable = { BRA_pres_support^24 = 1 }
		}

		# Jango becomes more popular due to Lott doesn't die
		if = {
			limit = {
				AND = {
					has_country_flag = BRA_lott_doesnt_die
					NOT = {
						has_country_leader = {
							character = BRA_Odilio_Denys
							ruling_only = yes
						}
					}
				}
			}
			add_to_variable = { BRA_pres_support^9 = 2 }
			add_to_variable = { BRA_pres_support^12 = 3 }
			add_to_variable = { BRA_pres_support^15 = 1 }
		}

		# Jango becomes less popular due to Denys coup
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_leader = {
					character = BRA_Odilio_Denys
					ruling_only = yes
				}
			}
			subtract_from_variable = { BRA_pres_support^3 = 2 }
			subtract_from_variable = { BRA_pres_support^6 = 2 }
			subtract_from_variable = { BRA_pres_support^18 = 2 }
			subtract_from_variable = { BRA_pres_support^21 = 2 }
			subtract_from_variable = { BRA_pres_support^24 = 2 }
		}
	}
	else = { # kubitschek
		# Add Kubitschek as the first candidate, he has id '1' and
		# is running with the PSD
		add_to_array = { BRA_pres_candidates = 1 }
		add_to_array = { BRA_pres_candidate_parties = PARTY_PSD }

		# Set up Kubitschek's support in the various regions
		# the raw numbers don't matter, this is just relative to the other candidates
		# Since Kubitschek is the first candidate, we start with 0, and then add 3 for each region
		# since there are 3 other candidates in the 1965 elections
		set_variable = { BRA_pres_support^0 = 53 }
		set_variable = { BRA_pres_support^3 = 42 }
		set_variable = { BRA_pres_support^6 = 33 }
		set_variable = { BRA_pres_support^9 = 40 }
		set_variable = { BRA_pres_support^12 = 53 }
		set_variable = { BRA_pres_support^15 = 37 }
		set_variable = { BRA_pres_support^18 = 35 }
		set_variable = { BRA_pres_support^21 = 29 }

		# Here we adjust Kubitschek's support based on the various events

		# Is Quadros running? if so Kubitschek loses support in Sao Paulo
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = BRA_65_quadros_candidate
			}
			set_variable = { BRA_pres_support^24 = 27 }
		}
		else = {
			set_variable = { BRA_pres_support^24 = 30 }
		}

		if = { # Jk becomes more popular
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = BRA_goulart_wins_hundred_days
			}
			add_to_variable = { BRA_pres_support^0 = 2 }
			add_to_variable = { BRA_pres_support^3 = 1 }
			add_to_variable = { BRA_pres_support^6 = 3 }
			add_to_variable = { BRA_pres_support^9 = 6 }
			add_to_variable = { BRA_pres_support^12 = 4 }
			add_to_variable = { BRA_pres_support^15 = 3 }
			add_to_variable = { BRA_pres_support^18 = 1 }
			add_to_variable = { BRA_pres_support^21 = 1 }
			add_to_variable = { BRA_pres_support^24 = 1 }
		}

		if = { # JK becomes more popular due to Lott doesn't die
			limit = {
				AND = {
					has_country_flag = BRA_lott_doesnt_die
					NOT = {
						has_country_leader = {
							character = BRA_Odilio_Denys
							ruling_only = yes
						}
					}
				}
			}
			add_to_variable = { BRA_pres_support^9 = 4 }
			add_to_variable = { BRA_pres_support^12 = 2 }
			add_to_variable = { BRA_pres_support^15 = 1 }
		}
	}

	if = { # quadros
		limit = { has_country_flag = BRA_65_quadros_candidate }

		# Add Quadros as the second candidate, he has id '2' and
		# is running with the UDN
		add_to_array = { BRA_pres_candidates = 2 }
		add_to_array = { BRA_pres_candidate_parties = PARTY_UDN }
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = brazil.606 days = 21 } }

		# Set up Quadros's support in the various regions
		# the raw numbers don't matter, this is just relative to the other candidates
		# Since Quadros is the second candidate, we start with 1, and then add 3 for each region
		# since there are 3 other candidates in the 1965 elections
		set_variable = { BRA_pres_support^1 = 34 }
		set_variable = { BRA_pres_support^4 = 33 }
		set_variable = { BRA_pres_support^7 = 44 }
		set_variable = { BRA_pres_support^13 = 34 }
		set_variable = { BRA_pres_support^16 = 33 }
		set_variable = { BRA_pres_support^19 = 43 }
		set_variable = { BRA_pres_support^22 = 38 }
		set_variable = { BRA_pres_support^25 = 30 }

		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = BRA_65_goulart_candidate
			}
			set_variable = { BRA_pres_support^10 = 36 }
		}
		else = {
			set_variable = { BRA_pres_support^10 = 28 }
		}

		if = { # Quadros becomes more popular
			limit = {
				has_country_leader = {
					character = BRA_Janio_Quadros
					ruling_only = yes
				}
			}
			add_to_variable = { BRA_pres_support^1 = 1 }
			add_to_variable = { BRA_pres_support^4 = 3 }
			add_to_variable = { BRA_pres_support^7 = 1 }
			add_to_variable = { BRA_pres_support^10 = 1 }
			add_to_variable = { BRA_pres_support^13 = 1 }
			add_to_variable = { BRA_pres_support^16 = 3 }
			add_to_variable = { BRA_pres_support^19 = 4 }
			add_to_variable = { BRA_pres_support^22 = 1 }
			add_to_variable = { BRA_pres_support^25 = 6 }
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = BRA_Quadros_has_passed_bill_10
					}
				}
				subtract_from_variable = { BRA_pres_support^1 = 1 }
				subtract_from_variable = { BRA_pres_support^4 = 1 }
				subtract_from_variable = { BRA_pres_support^7 = 1 }
				subtract_from_variable = { BRA_pres_support^10 = 1 }
				subtract_from_variable = { BRA_pres_support^13 = 1 }
				subtract_from_variable = { BRA_pres_support^16 = 1 }
				subtract_from_variable = { BRA_pres_support^19 = 1 }
				subtract_from_variable = { BRA_pres_support^22 = 1 }
				subtract_from_variable = { BRA_pres_support^25 = 1 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = BRA_Quadros_has_passed_bill_11
					}
				}
				subtract_from_variable = { BRA_pres_support^1 = 3 }
				subtract_from_variable = { BRA_pres_support^4 = 3 }
				subtract_from_variable = { BRA_pres_support^7 = 3 }
				subtract_from_variable = { BRA_pres_support^10 = 3 }
				subtract_from_variable = { BRA_pres_support^13 = 3 }
				subtract_from_variable = { BRA_pres_support^16 = 3 }
				subtract_from_variable = { BRA_pres_support^19 = 3 }
				subtract_from_variable = { BRA_pres_support^22 = 3 }
				subtract_from_variable = { BRA_pres_support^25 = 3 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = BRA_Quadros_has_passed_bill_12
					}
				}
				subtract_from_variable = { BRA_pres_support^1 = 1 }
				subtract_from_variable = { BRA_pres_support^4 = 1 }
				subtract_from_variable = { BRA_pres_support^7 = 1 }
				subtract_from_variable = { BRA_pres_support^10 = 1 }
				subtract_from_variable = { BRA_pres_support^13 = 1 }
				subtract_from_variable = { BRA_pres_support^16 = 1 }
				subtract_from_variable = { BRA_pres_support^19 = 1 }
				subtract_from_variable = { BRA_pres_support^22 = 1 }
				subtract_from_variable = { BRA_pres_support^25 = 1 }
			}
		}

		if = { # Quadros becomes more popular
			limit = {
				AND = {
					has_country_flag = BRA_lott_doesnt_die
					check_variable = { BRA_lottquadros_quadros_influence > 65 }
					NOT = {
						AND = {
							has_country_leader = {
								character = BRA_Odilio_Denys
								ruling_only = yes
							}
							has_country_flag = BRA_quadros_eats_shit_lmao_what_a_fucking_bitchass_fuck_you
						}
					}
				}
			}
			add_to_variable = { BRA_pres_support^4 = 1 }
			add_to_variable = { BRA_pres_support^16 = 1 }
			add_to_variable = { BRA_pres_support^19 = 2 }
			add_to_variable = { BRA_pres_support^25 = 4 }
		}

	}
	else = { # lacerda

		# Add Lacerda as the second candidate for the UDN
		add_to_array = { BRA_pres_candidates = 3 }
		add_to_array = { BRA_pres_candidate_parties = PARTY_UDN }

		# Set up Lacerda's support in the various regions
		# the raw numbers don't matter, this is just relative to the other candidates
		# Since Lacerda is the second candidate, we start with 1, and then add 3 for each region
		# since there are 3 other candidates in the 1965 elections

		set_variable = { BRA_pres_support^1 = 30 }
		set_variable = { BRA_pres_support^4 = 33 }
		set_variable = { BRA_pres_support^7 = 40 }
		set_variable = { BRA_pres_support^13 = 30 }
		set_variable = { BRA_pres_support^16 = 33 }
		set_variable = { BRA_pres_support^19 = 43 }
		set_variable = { BRA_pres_support^22 = 38 }
		set_variable = { BRA_pres_support^25 = 30 }

		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = BRA_65_goulart_candidate
			}
			set_variable = { BRA_pres_support^10 = 36 }
		}
		else = {
			set_variable = { BRA_pres_support^10 = 28 }
		}

		if = { # Lacerda becomes more popular
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = BRA_lacerda_wins_hundred_days
			}
			add_to_variable = { BRA_pres_support^1 = 1 }
			add_to_variable = { BRA_pres_support^4 = 2 }
			add_to_variable = { BRA_pres_support^7 = 1 }
			add_to_variable = { BRA_pres_support^10 = 1 }
			add_to_variable = { BRA_pres_support^13 = 1 }
			add_to_variable = { BRA_pres_support^16 = 3 }
			add_to_variable = { BRA_pres_support^19 = 4 }
			add_to_variable = { BRA_pres_support^22 = 6 }
			add_to_variable = { BRA_pres_support^25 = 1 }
		}
	}

	# Add Adhemar de Barros as the third candidate for the PSP
	add_to_array = { BRA_pres_candidates = 4 }
	add_to_array = { BRA_pres_candidate_parties = PARTY_PSP }

	# Set up Adhemar's support in the various regions
	# the raw numbers don't matter, this is just relative to the other candidates
	# Since Adhemar is the third candidate, we start with 2, and then add 3 for each region
	# since there are 3 other candidates in the 1965 elections
	set_variable = { BRA_pres_support^2 = 15 }
	set_variable = { BRA_pres_support^5 = 20 }
	set_variable = { BRA_pres_support^8 = 20 }
	set_variable = { BRA_pres_support^11 = 44 }
	set_variable = { BRA_pres_support^14 = 15 }
	set_variable = { BRA_pres_support^17 = 30 }
	set_variable = { BRA_pres_support^20 = 22 }
	set_variable = { BRA_pres_support^23 = 33 }
	set_variable = { BRA_pres_support^26 = 43 }

	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = BRA_65_goulart_candidate
		}
		set_variable = { BRA_pres_support^11 = 28 }
	}
	else = {
		set_variable = { BRA_pres_support^11 = 32 }
	}

	if = { # Adhemar becomes more popular
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = BRA_adhemar_wins_hundred_days
		}
		add_to_variable = { BRA_pres_support^2 = 1 }
		add_to_variable = { BRA_pres_support^5 = 2 }
		add_to_variable = { BRA_pres_support^8 = 1 }
		add_to_variable = { BRA_pres_support^13 = 1 }
		add_to_variable = { BRA_pres_support^14 = 1 }
		add_to_variable = { BRA_pres_support^17 = 1 }
		add_to_variable = { BRA_pres_support^20 = 2 }
		add_to_variable = { BRA_pres_support^23 = 1 }
		add_to_variable = { BRA_pres_support^26 = 8 }
	}

	if = {
		limit = {
			has_completed_focus = BRA_investigate_the_bull
		}
		subtract_from_variable = { BRA_pres_support^26 = 3 }
	}

	####################################
	# SETUP VARIOUS CAMPAIGNING ARRAYS #
	####################################

	# Size 27 because of 9 regions and 3 candidates
	resize_array = { array = BRA_pres_momentum size = 27 value = 0 }
	resize_array = { array = BRA_pres_infra size = 27 value = 1 }
	resize_array = { array = BRA_pres_fatigue size = 9 value = 1 }

	# Set up the campaigning party arrays
	# Size 9 for the 9 regions
	clear_array = BRA_pres_campaigning_party
	resize_array = { array = BRA_pres_campaigning_party size = 9 value = 0 }
	clear_array = BRA_pres_campaigning_party_2
	resize_array = { array = BRA_pres_campaigning_party_2 size = 9 value = 0 }

	############################################
	# MARK ELECTION ACTIVE, START AI CAMPAIGNS #
	############################################

	set_country_flag = BRA_pres_election_active

	BRA_redraw_pres_info = yes
	BRA_pres_select_region = yes

	BRA_pres_others_campaign = yes
	hidden_effect = {
		country_event = {
			id = brazil.252
			days = 7
		}
	}

	set_temp_variable = { alert_id = token:Alert_BRA_PresVoting }
	add_TNO_alert_unless_exists = yes
}

BRA_pres_start_70_election = {
	clear_array = BRA_pres_candidates
	clear_array = BRA_pres_candidate_parties
	clear_array = BRA_pres_support
	clear_array = BRA_pres_infra
	clear_array = BRA_pres_fatigue
	clear_array = BRA_pres_momentum
	clear_variable = BRA_pres_year

	set_variable = { BRA_pres_year = 1970 }

	BRA_initialize_pres_region_pop = yes

	set_temp_variable = { scenario = BRA_pres_70_scenario }

	if = {
		########################################################
		# SCENARIO 1: Vargas JR vs Edna/Brizola/Neves vs Braga #
		########################################################

		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				scenario = 1
			}
		}
