BRA_calc_military_expectations = {
	add_to_variable = { BRA_military_loyalty = BRA_military_drift }
	clear_variable = BRA_military_expectations_met
	clear_variable = BRA_military_drift
	#army manpower
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { global.SA_tension > 40 } }
		set_variable = { BRA_min_army_manpower = global.SA_tension }
		divide_variable = { BRA_min_army_manpower = 100 }
	}
	else = {
		set_variable = { BRA_min_army_manpower = 0.4 }
	}
	multiply_variable = { BRA_min_army_manpower = ARG.deployed_army_manpower_k }
	round_variable = BRA_min_army_manpower
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				check_variable = { BRA_min_army_manpower < BRA.deployed_army_manpower_k }
				check_variable = { BRA_min_army_manpower = BRA.deployed_army_manpower_k }
			}
		}
		add_to_variable = { BRA_military_expectations_met = 1 }
	}
	else = {
		add_to_variable = { BRA_military_drift = -0.25 }
	}

	#navy manpower
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { global.SA_tension > 75 } }
		set_variable = { BRA_min_navy_manpower = global.SA_tension }
		divide_variable = { BRA_min_navy_manpower = 100 }
	}
	else = {
		set_variable = { BRA_min_navy_manpower = 0.75 }
	}
	multiply_variable = { BRA_min_navy_manpower = ARG.deployed_navy_manpower_k }
	round_variable = BRA_min_navy_manpower
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				check_variable = { BRA_min_navy_manpower < BRA.deployed_navy_manpower_k }
				check_variable = { BRA_min_navy_manpower = BRA.deployed_navy_manpower_k }
			}
		}
		add_to_variable = { BRA_military_expectations_met = 1 }
	}
	else = {
		add_to_variable = { BRA_military_drift = -0.1 }
	}

	#air manpower
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { global.SA_tension > 75 } }
		set_variable = { BRA_min_air_manpower = global.SA_tension }
		divide_variable = { BRA_min_air_manpower = 100 }
	}
	else = {
		set_variable = { BRA_min_air_manpower = 0.75 }
	}
	multiply_variable = { BRA_min_air_manpower = ARG.deployed_airforce_manpower_k }
	round_variable = BRA_min_air_manpower
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				check_variable = { BRA_min_air_manpower < BRA.deployed_airforce_manpower_k }
				check_variable = { BRA_min_air_manpower = BRA.deployed_airforce_manpower_k }
			}
		}
		add_to_variable = { BRA_military_expectations_met = 1 }
	}
	else = {
		add_to_variable = { BRA_military_drift = -0.1 }
	}

	#army units
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { global.SA_tension > 50 } }
		set_variable = { BRA_min_army_units = global.SA_tension }
		divide_variable = { BRA_min_army_units = 100 }
	}
	else = {
		set_variable = { BRA_min_army_units = 0.5 }
	}
	add_to_variable = { BRA_min_army_units = 0.25 }
	multiply_variable = { BRA_min_army_units = ARG.num_divisions }
	round_variable = BRA_min_army_units
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				check_variable = { BRA_min_army_units < BRA.num_divisions }
				check_variable = { BRA_min_army_units = BRA.num_divisions }
			}
		}
		add_to_variable = { BRA_military_expectations_met = 1 }
	}
	else = {
		add_to_variable = { BRA_military_drift = -0.25 }
	}
}

BRA_update_agrarian_reform = { # why tf have we not done this yet, i hate you all and myself
	if = {
		limit = { has_idea = BRA_the_burning_farmland }
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = BRA_the_burning_farmland
			add_idea = BRA_countryside_strikes
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_idea = BRA_countryside_strikes }
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = BRA_countryside_strikes
			add_idea = BRA_latifundos_crisis
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_idea = BRA_latifundos_crisis }
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = BRA_latifundos_crisis
			add_idea = BRA_minor_agrarian_reform
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_idea = BRA_minor_agrarian_reform }
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = BRA_minor_agrarian_reform
			add_idea = BRA_radical_agrarian_reform
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_idea = BRA_radical_agrarian_reform }
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = BRA_radical_agrarian_reform
			add_idea = BRA_completed_agrarian_reform
		}
	}
}

BRA_upgrade_guanabara_dreaming = { # originally used dynamic modifiers, but apparently those dont work so you get this monstruosity instead. If anyone is brave enough to make this better, feel free # Challenge Accepted
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { guanabara_dynmod < 3 }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = GUANABARA_RECONSTRUCTION_FINISHED }
		}
		add_to_variable = { guanabara_dynmod = 1 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { guanabara_dynmod = 0 }
			has_country_flag = GUANABARA_RECONSTRUCTION_FINISHED
		}
		add_to_variable = { guanabara_dynmod = 1 }
		# Guanabara Dreaming Effects
		set_variable = { BRA_guanabara_state_production_speed_buildings_factor = 0.15 }
		set_variable = { BRA_guanabara_poverty_monthly_rate = 0.01 }
		force_update_dynamic_modifier = yes
		1488 = { force_update_dynamic_modifier = yes }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { guanabara_dynmod = 1 }
			has_country_flag = GUANABARA_RECONSTRUCTION_FINISHED
		}
		add_to_variable = { guanabara_dynmod = 1 }
		# Guanabara Dreaming Effects
		set_variable = { BRA_guanabara_state_production_speed_buildings_factor = 0.20 }
		set_variable = { BRA_guanabara_poverty_monthly_rate = 0.02 }
		set_variable = { BRA_guanabara_stability_factor = 0.02 }
		set_variable = { BRA_guanabara_free_production_units_modifier = 1 }
		force_update_dynamic_modifier = yes
		1488 = { force_update_dynamic_modifier = yes }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { guanabara_dynmod = 2 }
			has_country_flag = GUANABARA_RECONSTRUCTION_FINISHED
		}
		add_to_variable = { guanabara_dynmod = 1 }
		# Guanabara Dreaming Effects
		set_variable = { BRA_guanabara_state_production_speed_buildings_factor = 0.25 }
		set_variable = { BRA_guanabara_poverty_monthly_rate = 0.03 }
		set_variable = { BRA_guanabara_stability_factor = 0.04 }
		set_variable = { BRA_guanabara_free_production_units_modifier = 2 }
		set_variable = { BRA_guanabara_gdp_growth_modifier = 0.50 }
		set_variable = { BRA_guanabara_inflation_rate_modifier = -0.50 }
		force_update_dynamic_modifier = yes
		1488 = { force_update_dynamic_modifier = yes }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { guanabara_dynmod = 3 }
			has_country_flag = GUANABARA_RECONSTRUCTION_FINISHED
		}
		add_to_variable = { guanabara_dynmod = 1 }
		# Guanabara Dreaming Effects
		set_variable = { BRA_guanabara_state_production_speed_buildings_factor = 0.25 }
		set_variable = { BRA_guanabara_poverty_monthly_rate = 0.03 }
		set_variable = { BRA_guanabara_stability_factor = 0.05 }
		set_variable = { BRA_guanabara_free_production_units_modifier = 3 }
		set_variable = { BRA_guanabara_gdp_growth_modifier = 1.00 }
		set_variable = { BRA_guanabara_inflation_rate_modifier = -1.00 }
		set_variable = { BRA_guanabara_political_power_factor = 0.10 }
		set_variable = { BRA_guanabara_admin_efficiency_monthly_rate = 1.50 }
		force_update_dynamic_modifier = yes
		1488 = { force_update_dynamic_modifier = yes }
	}
}

BRA_adhemar_change_german_influence = {
	add_to_variable = { BRA_adhemar_german_influence = temp_adhemar_german_influence }
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { temp_adhemar_german_influence > 0 } }
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { temp_adhemar_german_influence = 1 } }
			custom_effect_tooltip = BRA_adhemar_increase_german_influence_small_tt
		}
		else = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = BRA_adhemar_increase_german_influence_tt
		}
	}
	else = {
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { temp_adhemar_german_influence = -1 } }
			custom_effect_tooltip = BRA_adhemar_decrease_german_influence_small_tt
		}
		else = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = BRA_adhemar_decrease_german_influence_tt
		}
	}
}

BRA_lacerda_ideology_change = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_government = paternalism
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = paternalism
			popularity = amount
		}
	}
	else = {
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = liberal_conservatism
			popularity = amount
		}
	}
}

BRA_calc_lacerda_campaign_trail_values = {
	add_to_variable = { BRA_lacerda_literacy_objective = BRA_illiteracy_array^0 }
	add_to_variable = { BRA_lacerda_literacy_objective = BRA_illiteracy_array^1 }
	add_to_variable = { BRA_lacerda_literacy_objective = BRA_illiteracy_array^2 }
	add_to_variable = { BRA_lacerda_literacy_objective = BRA_illiteracy_array^3 }
	add_to_variable = { BRA_lacerda_literacy_objective = BRA_illiteracy_array^4 }
	add_to_variable = { BRA_lacerda_literacy_objective = BRA_illiteracy_array^5 }
	add_to_variable = { BRA_lacerda_literacy_objective = BRA_illiteracy_array^6 }
	add_to_variable = { BRA_lacerda_literacy_objective = BRA_illiteracy_array^7 }
	add_to_variable = { BRA_lacerda_literacy_objective = BRA_illiteracy_array^8 }
	divide_variable = { BRA_lacerda_literacy_objective = 9 }

	set_variable = { BRA_lacerda_poverty_objective = BRA.poverty_rate }

	set_variable = { BRA_lacerda_gdp_objective = BRA.GDP }

	set_variable = { BRA_lacerda_northern_objective = BRA_develop_region_mech_rate^1 }

	set_variable = { BRA_lacerda_southern_objective = BRA_develop_region_industry^4 }
}

BRA_initialize_crise_petrolifera = {
	set_variable = { BRA_crise_petrolifera_interest_rate = 0 }
	set_variable = { BRA_crise_petrolifera_misc_income = 0 }
	set_variable = { BRA_crise_petrolifera_admin_efficiency	= 0 }
	set_variable = { BRA_crise_petrolifera_org_loss = 0.1 }
	set_variable = { BRA_crise_petrolifera_war_support = -0.05 }
	set_variable = { BRA_crise_petrolifera_fuel_gain = -0.2 }
	set_variable = { BRA_crise_petrolifera_consumer_goods = 0.05 }
	set_variable = { BRA_crise_petrolifera_factory_output = -0.05 }
	set_variable = { BRA_crise_petrolifera_construction_speed = -0.05 }
	set_variable = { BRA_crise_petrolifera_gdp_growth = -3 }
	add_dynamic_modifier = {
		modifier = BRA_crise_petrolifera_dynmod
	}

	# Non-Dynmod effects
	set_variable = { BRA_crise_petrolifera_inflation_change = 0.2 }
	set_temp_variable = { inflation_temp = BRA_crise_petrolifera_inflation_change }
	econ_inflation_change = yes

	set_variable = { BRA_crise_petrolifera_debt_monthly = 1 }
	set_temp_variable = { temp_econ_spending_amount = BRA_crise_petrolifera_debt_monthly }
	econ_spend_money_once_effect_raw_money = yes

	country_event = { # Monthly inflation, debt, and developmental effects
		id = brazil.596
		months = 1
	}
}

BRA_remove_crise_petrolifera = {
	remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = BRA_crise_petrolifera_dynmod }
	clear_variable = BRA_crise_petrolifera_interest_rate
	clear_variable = BRA_crise_petrolifera_misc_income
	clear_variable = BRA_crise_petrolifera_admin_efficiency
	clear_variable = BRA_crise_petrolifera_org_loss
	clear_variable = BRA_crise_petrolifera_war_support
	clear_variable = BRA_crise_petrolifera_fuel_gain
	clear_variable = BRA_crise_petrolifera_consumer_goods
	clear_variable = BRA_crise_petrolifera_factory_output
	clear_variable = BRA_crise_petrolifera_construction_speed
	clear_variable = BRA_crise_petrolifera_gdp_growth
	clear_variable = BRA_crise_petrolifera_inflation_change
	clear_variable = BRA_crise_petrolifera_debt_monthly
}
